1.juunengonoyakusoku

jumyouwokaitottemoraerutoiuhanashiwokiitatoki,oregamassakiniomoidashitanowa,shougakuseinokoroniuketadoutokunojugyounokotodatta.madajibundemonowokangaerutoiukotowoshiranaijuusainooretachinimukete,gakkyuutannnindearunijuudaikouhannojoseikyouinwa,konnnafuunitoikaketa.dehaminasanwa,souiufuunikakegaenonaimonodatoiwaretari,naniyorimokachinoarumonodatoiwaretarishiteiruningennoinochiwa,jissainokingakunisuruto,ikurakurainomonodatoomotteimasuka?sorekarakanojowa,chottokangaekomusoburiwomiseta.sonotoikatadewafujuubundato,jibundeomottanodarou.cho-kuwomottamamakokubantotaijishi,seitonisewomuketamamanijuubyouhodochinmokushiteita.sonokanmo,seitowashinkennikotaewokangaeteita.taihannoseitowasonowakakutekireinagakkyuutannningasukidattakara,nantokashitekanojonikiniirarerukotowoitte,homeraretakattanoda.ichininnoworikousanga,tewoageteitta.sarari-mannoheikintekinashougaichinginwaniokuenkarasanokuenhododato,konomaeyondahonnikaitearimashita.dakara,futsuunohitowa,daitaisorekuraidatoomoimasukyoushitsuniitaseitonohanbunwakanshinshitayounakaowoshita.mouhanbunwaomoshirokunasasounakaowoshita.hotondonoseitowa,sonoworikousannokotowokiratteita.gakkyuutannninwanigawaraiwoukabe,tashikani,sorewasounandesutoitteunazuita.otonanohitonikiitemo,tabun,onajikotaegakaettekurudeshoune.isshouotoushitekasegukingaku,soregasonohitonokachitoiko-runinarutoiukangaekatawa,hitotsunoseikaidatoierudeshou.tada,kokodewa,ichidosouiukangaekatawosutetehoshiindesu.aasoudesune,tatoehanashiwoshimashou.itsumono,wakarinikuitatoehanashikyouingaaonocho-kudekokubanniegaitamononoshoutaiwa,darenimowakaranakatta.ningennimomietashi,douronihebaritsuitagamunimomieta.demo,soregakanojononeraidatta.konoetainoshirenainanikawa,okanedakewa,ikurademomotteimasu.nanikawa,ningenrashiiseikatsuniakogareteimasu.souiuwakede,darekanojinseiwokaitoroutoshiteirundesu.aruhianatawa,guuzen,nanikanomaewotourisugarimasu.surutonanikagaanatani,koutoundesu.naa,kimigakorekaraokurujinseio,sokkurisonomamabokuniuttekurenaikai?tokanojowaittansokodehanashiwotomeru.sorewoutteshimauto,dounarundesuka?tokimajimesounaotokonokogatewoagetetazuneta.shindeshimaudeshounetokyouinwaheizentokotaeta.dakara,anatawananikanosasoio,ittanwakotowarudeshou.shikashi,nanikawakuisagarimasu.jaa,hanbundakedeiinda.kiminoyomeinorokujuunenkara,sanjuunenbundake,bokuniuttekurenaika.soregadoushitemohitsuyounandayohouzuewotsuitehanashiwokiiteitatoujinoorewa,naruhodonatoomotta.tashikani,sorekurainarautteyattemoiikigasuru.gendowaaruniseyo,hosokunagaijinseiyori,futokumijikaijinseinohougaiinikimatteirunoda.sate,kokokaragamondaidesu.kononingenrashiiseikatsuniakogarerunanikawa,anatanoyomeinitaishite,ichinennitsuki,ikurakurainonewotsuketekurerudeshou?aasakiniitteokimasuga,seikaiwaarimasenyo.anatatachigadonoyounikangaete,douittakotaewodasukagashiritaindesu.saa,shibaraku,chikakunosekinohitodoushidehanashiattemitekudasaikyoushitsugazawamekidasu.shikashi,orewahanashiainiwasankashinakatta.seikakuniiuto,dekinakatta.nazenaraoremo,sakihodoshougaichinginnohanashiwomochidashitaworikousandouyou,kurasunohanatsumamishadattakarada.hanashishiainikyoumiganaifuriwoshitsutsu,jikangasugirunowomatta.maenosekinorenchuuga,isshougasanokuenkuraidatosurutoaatoitteirunogakikoeta.aitsuragasanokuennara,toorewakangaeru.orewasanjuuokuenkuraiattemookashikunaina.hanashishiainokekkagadouittamonodattaka,orewaoboeteinai.fumounagironnishuushishiteitanowatashikada.somosomoshougakuseiniatsukaikireruyounakantannnate-madewanainoda.koukouseiwoatsumetatte,sorewoseisantekinagironnidekirukadoukawautagawashii.ikanimoshouraigakurasounaonnnanokoga,hitonoinochininedannantetsukerarenaitoatsukushuchoushiteitakotowa,yokuoboeteiru.tashikani,kanojotoonajijinseiwookurukenrigaarutoshitara,soreninewatsukanaidarousouorewaomotta.mushiro,shobunryoukinwoseikyuusarerunjanaidarouka.donokurasunimoichininwairuyounaatamanoiidoukewa,oretonitayounakotowokangaeteitarashiku,demobokutoonajijinseiwookurerukenrigautteitatoshitemo,kimitachi,sanhyakuenmoharawanainjanai?toittemawariwowarawaseteita.sonokangaekataniwasandoudekitaga,soitsugaakirakanijibunnokachigasokoraatarinokimajimenarenchuuyorimozuttotakaikotowojikakushitauede,shirajirashikujigyakutekinawaraiwotoroutoshiteirutokorowa,imaimashikukanjirareta.tokorode,gakkyuutannninwakonotoki,seikaiwanaitoitta.shikashiseikairashikimonowasonzaishita.juunengo,nijuusaininattaorewajissainijumyouwoutte,sonotaikawoerukotoninaru.kodomonokorowa,jibungaerainingenninarutoomotteita.dousedainoningentokurabete,jibunwanamihazureteyuushuunaningendatoomotteita.yakkainakotoni,orenosundeitachiikiniwa,doushiyoumonakusaenaioyanoundadoushiyoumonakusaenaikodomogaoukattakara,sonokanchigainihakushagakakarukotoninatta.orewamawarinokodomotachiwomikudashiteita.ogoriwokakushikireruhodokiyoudemokenkyodemonakattaorewa,touzen,kurasunominaniutomashigarareta.nakamahazurenisaretari,monowokakusaretarisurukotowamezurashikunakatta.tesutowaitsumomantenwototteitaga,soregadekitanowaoreichinindakedewanakatta.sou,reinoworikousannoonnnanoko,da.noseideorewahontounoimidenoichibanniwanarenakattashi,orenoseidewahontounoimidenoichibanniwanarenakatta.dakaraoretachiwa,sukunakutomohyoumentekiniwa,igamiatteitayouniomou.tsuneni,aitenouenitatsukotoshikakangaeteinakatta.shikashiippoude,otagaigayuiitsubanashinotsuujiruaitedearukotomotashikadatta.kochiranoiukotowogokainakuuketometekurerunowakanojodakedattashi,osorakumukounishitemosorewaonajikotodatta.souiuwakede,saishuutekiniwa,oretachiwaitsumoisshoniirukotoninarunodatta.motoyori,iegahobomamukainiarutoiukotode,osanaikorokaraoretachiwasoutounojikanwoisshonisugoshitekita.iwayuruosananajimitoiumononiatarunodarou.oyadoushinonakagayoku,shougakkounihairumadewa,kochiranoryoushingaisogashiitokiniwaorewamukounoieniazukerareteitashi,mukounoryoushingaisogashiitokiniwagakochiranoieniazukerareteita.tagaiwokyousouaitetoshikaminashiteinaioretachidattaga,oyanomaedewa,nakayokufurumaukotogaanmokunoryoukaidatta.koretoittariyuugaattawakedewanai.nantonaku,soushitahougayosasouniomoetadakeda.te-burunoshitadewahagiwokeriatarifutomomowotsuneriatarisuruyounakankeidattakeredomo,oyanomegaarutokinikagittewa,oretachiwakinookenaiosananajimidoushimitainishiteita.demo,hyottoshitara,hontounisoudattanokamoshirenai.momata,oretoonajiyounariyuude,kurasunorenchuunikirawareteita.jibunnoatamagaiitoomoikomi,shuuinoningenwomikudashi,sonotaidogaamarinirokotsudearutameni,kyoushitsudewanokemononisareteita.oretonoiewaokanochoujoufukinnitatteite,tanokurasumeitonoiekarawazuibunhanareteita.sorewatsugounoiikotodatta.oretachiwakyoriwoiiwakenishite,kurasumeitonoieniasobiniikazunijitakunihikikomorukotowoseitoukashita.doushiyoumonakutaikutsuninattatokidaketagainoiewootozure,sukidekokoniiruwakejanaitoittakaodefuhonnisouniasonda.Natsumatsurinohiyakurisumasuniwa,ryoushinniiranushinpaiwokakenaiyounininindegaishutsushiteburaburatojikanwotsubushitashi,oyakorekurie-shonyajugyousankannohiniwanakayoshinofuriwoshite,marudeninindakedeirunogaichibanrakudakara,sukikonondesoushiteirunodatodemoiufuunifurumatta.teinounakurasumeitonimuriwoittenakamaniiretemorauyoriwa,nikutarashiiosananajimitoiruhougazuttomashidatoomottanoda.shougakkouwa,oretachinitottekinomeirubashodatta.tabitabi,oreyanitaisuruiyagarasegamondaininattegakkyuukaigigahirakareta.yonnenseikararokunenseimadetannnindattajoseikyouinwa,konotenomondainirikaigaatte,yohodohidoikotoninaranaikagiriwa,souittakotowooretachinoryoushinnirenrakushinaideitekureta.sonotouri,ryoushinnimadeijimerarekkodearukotowoshiraretara,iyoiyooretachinotachibawaketteitekinamonotonatteshimau.tattaichikashodakedemo,jibuntachigaijimerarekkodearukotowowasuresasetekurerubashogahitsuyoudearukotoo,sonojoseikyouinwayokuwakatteita.shikashinaniniseyo,itsudatteoretowaunzarishiteita.mawarinorenchuunitaishitemosoudashi,mawaritosouiukankeishikakizukenaijibunnitaishitemo,kokoronosumideusuusuunzarishiteita.oretachinitotteichibannomondaiwa,umakuwaraenakattakotoda.minagaisseiniwarauyounataimingude,isshoniwaraukotogadekinakatta.murinikaonokinnnikuwougokasoutosuruto,jibunnonakaniarukanjinnnabubunga,garigaritokezurareruotogashita.monitayounakotowokanjiteitanodarou.douchounowaraiwoshiiruyounafunnikinonakademo,oretachiwamayuhitotsuugokasanakatta.ugokasenakatta,toittemoii.sonnnaoretachio,kyoushitsunorenchuuwa,takabishadatokakidoriyadatokaittekeibetsushiteita.tashikanioretachiwatakabishade,kidoriyadattadarou.shikashi,mawariniawaseteumakuwaraenakattanowa,soredakegagennindewanainoda.mottokonpontekinatokorode,oretowaketteitekinizureteita.sakukisetsuwomachigaetahananoyouni.juusainonatsunokotodatta.nanijuukaitogomibakonisuteraretakabanwoseottato,desakemewoireraretakutsuwohaitaorewa,yuuyakeniterasaretajinjanoishidannisuwatte,nanikawomatteita.oretachinoichikarawa,Natsumatsurinokaijougamioroseta.semaisandouniyataigagisshiritonarabi,niretsunochouchingakassourotounoyounimassugutsuzuki,usuguraikeidaiwoakakuterashiteiru.ikikauhitobitowaminajoukigennnayousude,dakarakosooretachiwa,sokonioriteikukotowadekinakatta.tagainidamarikondeitanowa,kuchiwoakeba,sonokoeganijindeshimaukotogawakatteitakarada.oretachiwakuchiwokitsukumusunde,gamanzuyokusokonisuwatteita.oretogamatteitanowa,jibuntachinosonzaiwokouteishitekureru,subetewonattokusasetekureru,nanikadatta.higurashinokoegafurisosogujinjade,nininwasukunakarazu,kaminiinotteitanokamoshirenai.himoochikaketakoro,wafuinitachiagari,suka-tonoyogorewotedeharatte,massugushoumenwomisuetamamaitta.watashitachiwashourai,tottemoerakunarundayokanojodakegamotsu,anosukitouttakoede.marude,tattaimakakuteishitajijitsuwoiukanoyouni.aashouraitte,dorekuraisakinohanashi?toorewakikikaeshita.sonnnanichikaihanashijanaitoomou.demo,sonnnanitouihanashidemonai.tabun,juunengokuraijuunengotoorewakurikaesu.sonokoroniwaoretachiwanijuusaidajuusainooretachinitotte,nijuusaitoiunenreiwadainootonawoimishiteita.dakaraoreniwa,nosonokotobawa,sokosokogenjitsutekidearuyouniomoeta.watsuzuketa.sou,sononanikawakitto,natsuniokoruno.juunengononatsu,watashitachinitottemoiikotogaokite,sonotokiwatashitachiwa,youyakuikiteteyokattattekokoronosokokaraomoeruno.erakunatte,wokanemochininattawatashitachiwa,shougakuseidattakorowofurikaette,kouiunda.anoshougakkouwa,watashitachininanimoataetekurenakatta.doitsumokoitsumomanukebakaride,hanmenkyoushinisuranaranakatta.tonikaku,hidoishougakkoudattattesoudana.hontounimanukebakkaridatta.hontounihidoigakkoudattatoorewaitta.sonoshitenwa,toujinoorekarasuruto,kanarizanshindatta.shougakuseinitotteshougakkoutoiunowasekainosubetede,sokoniyoshiashigaarutoiufuuniwa,nakanakakangaerarenaimonoda.dakarajuunengoniwa,watashitachiwatottemoeraku,wokanemochininatteiruhitsuyougaaruno.imanokurasumeitoga,minnnashittodeshinzouhossawookosukurainishittodekuchibiruwokamisenkirukurainitoorewadouishita.soujanaito,wariniawanaimonnetokanojowahohoenda.orewasoreo,kiyasumetowaomotteinakatta.nokuchikarakiitatotan,orewasorega,hontounikakuteishitamiraidearukanoyounikanjita.sonokotobawayogennoyounihibiita.soudayona,oretachigaerakunarenaiwakeganaijanaika.juunengo,oretachiwaaitsurawomikaeshiteyarunda.konnnafuunimugeniatsukatteitakotoo,shinuhodokoukaisaseteyaru.aasorenishitemo,nijuusaitte,sugoinetowaii,ryoutewoushironitsuiteyuuyakesorawomiageta.juunengoniwanijuusaikasakeganomeru.tabakogasueru.kekkongadekirunowa,mottomaekarakatoorewaitta.soudane.onnnanokowajuurokusaikarakekkondekiruotokowajuuhachisaikaraka.demoorewa,itsumademokekkondekinaikigasurunadoushite?kirainamonogaousugirunda.yononakaniokorukotogananimokamoiyananda.sonnnande,yattekeruwakeganaiyosoka.jaa,watashimosoukamosouitte,wautsumuku.yuuhinisomarukanojonoyokogaowa,itsumotowabetsujinnoyounimieta.yoriotonabitemietashi,yorikizutsukiyasusounimomieta.aanee,sorejaasatoittewaoretotsukanomamewoawase,sugunisorashita.nijuusaininatte,watashitachigaerakunatteaamoshisonotoki,otagai,nasakenaikotoni,kekkonsuruyounaaitegamitsukattenakattatoshitarachiisakusekiwoshitekara,kanojowaiu.sonotokiwa,urenokoridoushi,isshoninarimasenka?totsuzenkuchougakawattanogahajiratteiruakashidatoiukotowa,toujinoorenimowakatta.nandesuka,sorewatooremoteineinikaeshita.aajoudandayo.wasuretechoudaitowachakasuyouniwaratta.ittemitadake.watashigaurenokoruhazuganaikaranesoitsuwayokatta,tooremowaratta.shikashihijounibakagetahanashidakeredotohanarebanareninattanochidemo,orewasonoyakusokuwoitsumademooboeteita.dakara,sorenarinimiryokutekinaonnnanokonikouiwoshimesaretemo,hakkiritokyohishita.chuugakuseininattemo.koukouseininattemo.daigakuseininattemo.itsukakanojotosaikaishitatoki,chantourenokotteirusugatawomiserareruyouni.mattakumotte,bakagetahanashidatoomou.anokorokara,juunengasugita.katsutewofurikaette,orewaomou.arewaarede,kagayakashiijidaidattanokamoshirenai,to.

2.owarinohajimari

sonohijuukyuukaimenomoushiwakegozaimasenwoittefukabukatoatamawosagetaorewa,sonomamamemaiwookoshiteyukanitaorekondeatamawouchi,ishikiwoushinattarashikatta.biaga-dendearubaitowoshiteitasaichuunokotodatta.genninwawakarikitteita.hotondoshokujimosezunientenkadehatarakitsuzuketeireba,daredemosounaru.muriwoshiteichinindeapa-tonimodottanochi,menookugaegurareruyouniitandanode,kekkyokubyouinniikukotonishita.takushi-dekyuukyuugairainiittakotode,tadadesaeayaukattaorenofutokorojijouwa,saraniakkashita.kuwaete,tenchounishibarakushigotowoyasumuyouniiwareteshimatta.mataseikatsuwokiritsumenakerebanarazu,shikashikoreijounaniwokiritsumerebaiinokawakaranakatta.saigoninikuwotabetanogaitsudattakamoomoidasenai.yonkagetsumokamiwokitteinakattashi,issakunennofuyuniko-towokatteirai,fukuwaichichakumokatteinakatta.daigakunihaittekaradarekatoasobiniittakotowaichidomonai.oyaniwatayorenaijijougaatta.sounaruto,dounikajibundekinwotsukurushikanai.shi-ji-tohonwotebanasunowa,kokorogaitanda.izuremochuukohinde,genseinashinasadamenosuenikounyuushitamonodattaga,pasokonmoterebimonaiorenoheyade,imayakinninarisounamonowakoredakedatta.wowakarewosurumaeni,semeteshi-ji-dakewaichidosubetekikitoushiteokukotonishita.heddohonwoshite,tataminiyokotawari,pureiya-nosaiseibotanwoosu.risaikurushoppudekattaaoihanenosenpuukinosuitchiwoire,teikitekinidaidokorodekoppunireisuiwososoidenonda.daigakuwoyasumunowahajimetedatta.daga,oregainakunattatokorodedaremokinishinaidarou.yasundakotosaekizukareteinaikamoshirenai.ichimai,mataichimai,tsumiageraretashi-ji-ga,miginotoukarahidarinotouheidoushiteitta.kisetsuwanatsude,orewanijuusaidattaga,katsutePo-Runizangaittatouri,nijuusaitoiunenreiwa,kanarazushimohitonoisshoudeichibanutsukushiinenreidearutowakagiranai.juunengononatsu,watashitachinitottemoiikotogaokite,sonotokiwatashitachiwa,youyakuikiteteyokattattekokoronosokokaraomoerunotoiunoyogenwa,hazureta.sukunakutomoorenohouniwaimanotokoroiikotowaokiteinaishi,kongookirukehaimonai.mukouwaimananiwoyatteirundarou,toorewakangaeru.shougakuyonnenseinonatsunikanojogatenkoushitehanarebanareninattekarawa,ichidomoatteinakatta.konnnahazudewa,nakatta.demo,sorewasoredeyokattanokamoshirenai.chuugaku,koukou,daigakutoshingakusurunitsure,chakujitsuniheibondetaikutsunaningenninatteikusugatao,kanojonimirarezunisundanodakara.dagaippoude,koukangaerukotomodekiruosananajimigaoretoonajichuugakunikitekureteitara,orewakonnnakotoniwanaranakattanokamoshirenai.kanojogatonariniitakoronoorewa,tsuneni,yoiimideharitsumeteita.oregananikanasakenaikotowosurebakanojoniwarawarerushi,oregananikasuguretakotowosurebakanojogakuyashigattekureru,souiukinchoukangaattakarakoso,toujinoorewajibunwosaikounojoutainimotteiketeitanokamoshirenai.kokosuunenkan,orewasonnnafuuni,koukaibakarishiteita.anokoronooregaimanoorewomitara,ittainaniwoomoudarou?sannichikankaketetaihannoshi-ji-wokikioetaorewa,hontounitaisetsunasuumaidakenokoshite,nochiwanokorazukamibukuronishimatta.mouhitotsunokamibukuroniwa,sudenihongagisshiritotsumeteatta.soreraworyouteniburasage,orewamachinideta.hinoshitawoaruiteiruuchini,miminarigashitekita.seminofukisokunanakigoekarakurusakkakukamoshirenai.marudemimimotodenakareteirukanoyoudatta.sonokoshotenwohajimeteotozuretanowa,ichinenmaenonatsu,oregadaigakunihaittesuukagetsunokorodatta.madamachinochirigaatamanihaitteinakattaorewa,sonohimomichinimayoi,ichijikanchikakumojibungadokowoaruiteirunokahaakudekiteinaijoukyougatsuzuiteita.rojiwonuketekaidanwonobottasakide,orewasonokoshotenwomitsuketa.igo,nandomosonokoshotenniikoutoshitanodaga,doushitemobashogawakaranakatta.shirabeyoutoshitemo,itsumotenmeiwowasureteshimau.tamatamamichinimayottatoki,guuzensokonitadoritsuku,toiunogatsunedatta.marudesonokoshotennitsuujirumichiga,kimagurenisugatawodashitarikeshitarishiteirukanoyouni.mayowazuikeruyouninattanowakotoshinihaittekarada.misesakini,itsunomanikaasagaogasaiteita.shuukande,hyounideteiruyasumonoyounohondananonakaminihenkaganaikawotashikametanochi,orewamisenihaitta.tatemonononakawausuguraku,furuikaminonioigajuumanshiteite,okunohoukarawarajionootogakikoetekita.karadawoyokonisurukotodedounikatourerukurainosemaitsuurowonuke,orewatenshunikoewokaketa.tsumiageraretahonnosukimakara,shiwadarakenoroujingaokkuusounikaowodasu.koshotennotenshudearukonoroujinwa,aitegadaredearoutoegaotoiumonowomattakumisenai.kaikeinotokiwa,itsudemoshitawomuitamamabosobosotonedanwoyomiagerudakeda.shikashikonohiwachigatta.oregahonwourinikitatoiuto,mezurashikukaowoagete,orenomewomitanoda.roujinnokaoniwa,tashikaniodorokinoyounamonogamiukerareta.maa,karenokimochiwawakaranaidemonai.oregauroutoshiteitahonwaizuremo,tatoenankaiyomitousouto,temotonioiteokukachinoaruhondatta.sorewotebanasunadotoiunowa,aruteidohonwoyomuningenkarasuruto,rikaishigataikoudounanodarou.hikkoshidemosurunoka?tokarewaorenikiita.igainimo,yokutourukoedatta.ie,souiuwakedewanaindesujaatoittekarewatemotonitsumiageraretahonwomiorosu.doushitekonnnamottainaikotowosuru?kamiwashokukanmowaruishi,eiyoumoarimasenkararoujinwaorenojoudanworikaishitekuretayoudatta.kinketsukatokarewakuchiwomageteitta.oregashukousuruto,karewananikakangaekomuyouniudewokundeshibarakuchinmokushiteitaga,omoinaoshitayouniikiwofuttohaki,sateiniwasanjuufunkuraikakarutodakeii,honwokakaetemisenookunihikkonda.sotonidetaorewa,michibatanofuruikeijibanwonagameteita.natsumatsuri,hotarunokanshoukai,tentaikansoku,dokushokainikansuruposuta-gaharareteita.heiwohasandamukougawakarawa,senkoutotataminonioi,soreniseikatsushuuyakinokaorigamajiriatta,anonatsukashiinioigashita.dokokatoukunoiede,fuuringanatteita.sateigaowari,kochiragasouteishiteitagakunosanbunnnoniteidowoorenitewatashitaroujinwa,naatoitta.hitotsu,hanashigaarundanandeshou?omae,kinnikomatterundarou?imanihajimattakotojaarimasenkedoneoregaaimainikotaeruto,roujinwakatteninattokushitayouniunazuku.maa,omaegadorekuraibinbounanokatoka,doushitebinbouninattanokatoka,souiukotoniorewakyoumiganai.oregaomaenikikitaikotowa,tadahitotsudaroujinwaichihakuoite,iu.jumyouwourukiwaneeka?fushizennnatangonokumiawaseni,orenohannnouwaichimawariokureta.jumyou?toorewakakuninnoimiwokometekikikaeshita.aa, dakeshiawaseninatari,hitowoshiawasenishitari,yumewokanaetari,shakainikoukenshitarisurukotoninatteitaka,toittakijunwomotonisateigakuwokimeteirutoiukotodesusonokouseisaga,saraniorewouchinomesu.tannnishiawaseninarenakatari,tannnihitowoshiawasenidekinakatari,tannniyumewokanaerarenakatari,tannnishakaikoukendekinakataritannnidorekahitotsunokijunnioitemukachidearutoiudakenara,madaii.shikashi,shiawaseninarezu,katsudaremoshiawasenidekizu,katsuyumewokanaerarezu,katsushakainikoukendekinaitoiukotoninarutoorewadokonisukuiwomiidasebaiinoka,wakaranakunatteshimau.kasanete,sanjuunentoiu,nijuusainishitewaisasakamijikasugiruyomei.taibyoudemowazuraunodarouka?jikonidemoaunodarouka?nazeorewakonnnaniyomeigamijikainda?toorewadamemotodekiitemiru.moushiwakearimasengatoonnnatenninwachiisakuatamawosageru.koreyorisakinojouhouwa,jikan,kenkou,jumyounoizurekawoouriitadaitaokyakusamanominishikakoukaidekinaikotoninatteorimasumikenwoosaetamama,orewakangaekonda.sukoshi,kangaesasetekuregoyukkuridouzotokanojowakotaetaga,sonokuchoukaraitte,sassatokimetehoshisoudatta.kekkyokuorewa,sankagetsudakenokoshite,nokorinosanjuunensubetewouriharatta.arubaitozukenoseikatsuyafuruhonnyatoshi-ji-shoppudenodekigotoniyotte,orewajishinnizokusurumonoyajikanwoyasuurisurukotoniteikouganakunatteshimatteita.onnnatenninkarakeiyakushononakamiwochikuichikakuninsareteiruma,orewahotondonanimokangaezuniaizuchiwokurikaeshiteitadakedatta.nanikashitsumonwanaikatotazuneraretemo,tokuninaitokotaeta.sassatoowarasete,deteikitakattanoda.konomisekaramo.konojinseikaramo.baibaiwa,goukeidesankaimadeokonaukotogadekimasutoonnnatenninwaitta.atonikai,anatawa,jumyoukenkoujikannobaibaiwookonaerutoiukotodesusanjuumanennohaittafuutouwouketotte,orewamisewodeta.soregadouyatteokonawaretakawakentoumotsukanainodaga,jumyouwoushinattakankakuwa,tashikaniatta.soremadeshintainoshinnitsumatteitananikaga,kyuuwarikatanukitorareteshimattayoudatta.atamawokiriotosaretaniwatorinodoutaigashibarakuwagenkinihashirimawatteirukotogaarurashiiga,kankakutoshitewasorenichikai.mohayashitaitoyondemoiiyounajoutainanoda.nijuuichisaininarezunishinukotogahobokakuteishitaorenoshintaiwa,hachijuunenwoikirutsumorideitashintaitowachigatte,sekkachinayoudatta.nanigenaiichibyounoomomigamashiteita.hachijuunenikirutsumorideitatokinooreniwa,doushitemoatorokujuunenmoarutoiumanshingamuishikiniattayoudaga,nokorisankagetsutomonaruto,nanikashinakerebanaranaitoiushousoukanniosowareta.towaie,kyouwahitomazukaettenemuritakatta.achikochiarukimawatte,kutakutanitsukarekitteita.kongonitsuitekangaeruniwa,kokoroyukumadenete,kimochiyokuokitanochinishitakatta.kaerimichi,orewakimyounaotokotosurechigatta.nijuudaizenhannimierusonootokowa,manmennoemiwotatae,tanoshikuteshouganaitoittayousude,ichinindearuiteita.mushouni,haragatatta.shoutengainosakayanitachiyottekanbi-ruwoyonhonkai,oriyokumitsuketayataideyakitoriwogohonkai,sorerawonomikuishinagarakaetta.yomeisankagetsu.moukinniitomewotsukeruhitsuyouwanai.aruko-ruwosesshusurunowahisashiburidatta.kibungaochikondeitanomo,yokunakattanokamoshirenai.okagedeattoiumaniyoigamawari,meiteishi,kitakushitesanjuufuntoshinaiuchinihakuhameninatta.koushiteorenosaigonosankagetsugahajimaru.suta-tonokirikatatoshitewa,saiakunichikai.

3.sankakuzuwarinokanshiin

tadadesaekibungawaruinoni,atsukutenegurushiiyorudatta.okagedesaibumadekukkiritoshitayumewomita.mewosamashitanochimo,orewasonoyumewofutonnonakadehansuusuru.iyanayumedewanai.soredokoroka,shiawasenayumedatta.shikashishiawasenayumehodozankokunamonomonai.yumenonakanoorewakoukouseide,butaiwakouendatta.orenoshitteirukouendewanakattaga,sokoniitanowashougakkoujidainodousouseidatta.douyaradousoukaigaokonawareteirutoiusetteinoyumerashii.mina,hanabiwotenitanoshisounishiteita.hibananiterasaretakemurigaakakusomaru.orewakouennosotonitatteite,karerawonagameteita.koukouseikatsuwadou?to,itsunomanikatonariniitagaorenikiita.kanojowoyokomenimiyoutoshitaga,sonokaowaboyaketeita.orewajuusaiyorisakinokanojowoshiranakattakara,umakusouzoudekinakattanodarou.shikashi,yumenonakanoorewa,nokaowokokorokarakireidatoomotta.kanojotofurukukaranoshiriaidearukotoo,hokorashikuomotta.tanoshimeteirutowaienaina,toorewashoujikinikotaeta.demo,saiakuttehododemonai.watashimosonnnatokorokana,towaunazuku.kanojogajibuntoonajiyounimijimenaseishunwosugoshiteirukotoo,orewahisokaniureshikuomou.imaninatteomoundakedosa,tokanojowaiu.anokorowa,kittotanoshikattandane.donokorowoitterunda?toorewakikikaesu.toiniwakotaezu,washagamikonde,orewomiageteiu.wa,madaurenokotteruno?maana,toorewakotaetsutsu,kanojonohyoujounimewokorasu.hannnouwotashikameru.soka,towaakirewaraiwoukaberu.maa,watashimosounandakedo.sorekara,hanikandayounahyoujoude,koutsuketashita.yokatta.junchoudane.aa,junchouda,toorewadouisuru.sonnnayumeda.nijuusaininattemiruyumedewanakatta.nanitekodomojimitayumedarou,toorewajikokennosuru.shikashidoujini,sonoyumewokenmeinikiokushiteokoutoshiteirujibungairu.wasureteshimauniwaoshiikara.juusainokoro,oreganokotowotaishiteyoiteinakattakotowatashikada.kanojonitaishitemotteitakouiwa,honnnowazukanamonodatta.mondaiwa,soushitahonnnowazukanakouisae,orewagonideattadarenitaishitemoidakukotogadekinakattatoiukotoda.hyottosuruto,anoikkenchiisanakouiwa,orenojinseinioitewasaidainomonodattanjanaikasorenikizuitanowa,kanojogainakunatta,zuttogodatta.noyumewonyuunennisaibumadekiokushitaorewa,sonomamafutonnonakade,kinounodekigotonitsuitekangaeteita.anofuruboketabirude,orewajumyouwosankagetsudakenokoshiteuriharatteshimatta.omoikaesutohakuchuumunoyouda,towaomowanakatta.sonodekigotowa,orenonakadekakkotoshitariarithiwotamotteita.ikioidejumyounotaihanwouriharatteshimattakotowokoukaisuru,toiukotomonakatta.ushinattehajimetesonotaisetsusanikizukutoiukotomonai.mushiro,katanonigaoriteseiseishitatoiukangatsuyokatta.koremadeorewonamanitsunagitometeitanowa,hyottoshitara,itsukaiikotogaarukamoshirenaitoiuasahakanakitaidatta.ikuramukonkyonakitaitowaie,sorewosutekirunowashinannogoudatta.donnnamukachinaningendarouto,subetenofuunwochoukeshinisurukurainokouunnimegumarenaitoiuhoshouwa,dokonimonainoda.sorewasukuideari,doujiniwanademoatta.dakarakoso,konkai,kongo,omaenojinseiniiikotowaokoranaitodangenshitemoraetakotowa,mikataniyottewaarigataikotodatta.korede,anshinshiteshinukotogadekiru.kounatteshimattakaraniwa,semetenokorinosankagetsudakewa,tanoshikusugoshitaimonoda.saenaijinseidattaga,shiwokakugoshitekaranosankagetsudakewa,sorenarinikoufukudatta,saigonisouomoeruyounayoseiwosugoshitai.mazuhashotenniittezasshidemoyomi,korekarasubekikotonitsuitekangaeyoutoorewakimetesonotoki,yobiringanatta.darekagatazunetekuruyoteiwanakatta.sonnnamonowakokosuunenkanichidomonaishi,kongosankagetsumosoudarou.heyanomachigaika,shuukinka,kannyuuka.izureniseyoiiyokanwashinakatta.yobiringafutatabinatta.futonwodetetachiagattaorewa,totanni,sakubannoyounatsuyoihakikeniosowareta.futsukayoida.soredemonantokagamanshitegenkanniikidoawoakeruto,sokonitatteitanowa,mishiranuonnnanokodatta.katawaraniwakanojonomonorashiiKyari-ke-sugaatta.aadochirasama?toorewatazuneta.kanojowaakiretayounakaowoshitanochi,okkuusounikabankaratoridashitameganewokake,korededaredakawakattadarou,todemoiitagenikochirawomita.sokodeorewa,youyakukizuku.kinou,orenojumyouwosateishitaaasoudesutoonnnanokowaitta.su-tsunoinshoubakarigakiwadatteitanode,shifukusugatanokanojowamarudebetsujinnimieta.kottonnoburausuni,sakkusuburu-nodangari-suka-to.kinouwaushirodemusundeitanodewakaranakattaga,katamadenonagasagaarukurokaminiwa,yuruiuchimakinokusegaatta.sakihodokaketemorattameganegoshinimieruhitomiwa,kokoronashikaureiwoobiteiruyounimomieru.suka-tokaranobiruhosoiashinimewoyaruto,migihizanioukimenobansoukougahatteatta.soutoufukaikizurashiku,bansoukounouekarademokizunojoutaigawakatta.shotaimendewajuuhachisaikaranijuuyonsaitoimaichinenreiwoshiborikirenakattaga,kyounokanojowomitemeboshigatsuita.osorakuoretoonajikuraidarou.juukyuuka,nijuutoiutokoroda.sorenishitemo,nazekanojoga,kokoniirunodarou?massakiniomoitsuitariyuuwa,sateikekkaniayamarigaattakotowotsutaenikitatoiumonodatta.jitsuhaketawomachigaeteita.moshikuhatanohitonokekkatotorichigaeteita.kanojowasonoshazainikitanokamoshirenai,toorewakitaisezuniwairarenakatta.onnnanokowafutatabimeganewohazushi,kichoumennike-sunishimai,futatabiorewokanjounonaimedemitsumeta.kyoukarakanshiinwotsutomesaseteitadaku,desusouiuto,tonanoruonnnanokowaorenikarukueshakushita.kanshiin.sukkariwasureteita.sonnnahanashimoattana,toorewakinounotonokaiwawoomoidashitsutsu,hakikenitaerarenakunaritoirenikakekondehaita.inonakamiwoichitouridashikittekaratoirewoderuto,doanosugumaenigatsutatteita.shigototowaie,enryononaionnnanokoda.orewakanojowooshinokeruyounishitesenmenshoniiki,kaowoaratteugaiwoshi,koppudemizuwogabunomishitanochi,futatabifutonniyokotawatta.hidoizutsuudatta.mushiatsusagasorewojochoushiteita.kinoumosetsumeisaseteitadakimashitakeredoitsunomanikaorenomakuramotonitatteitagaitta.anatanoyomeiwaichinenwokirimashitanode,kyoukarawajouji,kanshigatsukukotoninarimasu.tsukimashitewaaasonohanashi,mousukoshigonishitekurenaika?toorewarokotsuniiradachiwokometeitta.mitenotouri,guaigawaruindawakarimashita.dewa,gonishimasusouiuto,waKyari-ke-suwomotteheyanosuminiiki,kabenisewomuketesankakusuwariwoshita.sonogowa,tadahitasuraorenokotowonagameteita.douyara,oregaheyaniirumawa,sokokarakanshiwosurutsumorirashii.watashinokotowa,inaitoomotteitadaitekekkoudesukaratowaheyanosumikaraitta.douzookininasarazu,itsumotouri,nobinobitoseikatsushitekudasaishikashi,souiwaretatokorode,toshigafutatsutohanareteinaionnnanokonikanshisareteirutoiujijitsunikawariwanai.orewadoushitemokininatte,noiruhouwochiraritonusumimita.no-toninanikakakikondeiruyouda.kanshikirokunoyounamonowotsuketeirunokamoshirenai.ippoutekinikansatsusarerunowa,fuyukaidatta.kanojonimirareteirugawanohanshinga,hirihiritoshisendeyakeruyouda.kanshiinnitsuitewa,tashikanikinounojitendekuwashiisetsumeiwouketeita.nohanashiniyoruto,anomisedejumyouwouttahitonooukuga,hanatteokuto,yomeiichinenwokittakorokarajiboujikininatte,mondaikoudouwookosuyouninarunodasouda.mondaikoudounogutaitekinanaiyounitsuitekuwashikuwakikanakattaga,daitaiyosouwatsuku.hitogakisokuwomamorunowa,ikitsuzukeruuede,shinnyoutoiumonogaoukinakagiwonigitteirukarada.daga,jinseigamamonakuowarutoiukotogakakuteishiteirunodeareba,hanashiwakawattekuru.shinnyouwaanoyomadewamotteikerumonodewanai.jumyouwouttaningengajiboujikininaritashanikigaiwokuwaerutoiujitaiwofusegutamenidekitashisutemuga,konokanshiinseidonanodasouda.yomeiichinenwokittamononiwakanshigatsukerare,futekisetsunakoudougamiraretabaai,sokuzanikanshiinkarahonbunirenrakugaiki,honrainojumyoutowakankeinashini,sonobadejumyouwotsukisaserarerunodatoiu.heyanosuminisankakusuwarishiteiruanoonnnanokowa,denwaichihondeorenoinochiwoubaerutoiukotoda.tadakorewatoukeitekiniyuuinakekkagashimesaretakarasoushiteirurashiinodagashimadenokorisuunichitoiutokoromadekuruto,hitowataninnimeiwakuwokakeyoutoiukiganakunarunodasouda.soreyueni,yomeiganokorisannichitonattatoki,kanshiingahazusarerurashii.saigonosannichikandakewa,ichininninarerunoda.itsunomanikanemutteshimatteitarashikatta.megasameruto,zutsuutohakikewakieteita.tokeiwagogonanajihodowosashiteita.kichounasankagetsunosaishonoichinichinosugoshikatatoshitewa,hobosaiakutoitteii.waaikawarazu,heyanosumidejittoshiteita.narubekukanojowoishikishinaiyounishite,itsumotourikoudousurukotowokokorogakeru.reisuidekaowoarai,heyagiwonugi,sukkariiroochishitaburu-ji-nzutosusonohotsuretathi-shatsunikigae,yuushokuwokainisotohedeta.kanshiinnowa,orenogohohodoushirowotsuitekita.aruiteiruto,tsuyoinishibinimegakuranda.konohinoyuuyakewakiirokatta.toukunohayashikarahigurashinonakigoegakikoeru.hodounowakiniarusenroo,tankounosharyougakedarusounihashirinuketeitta.kyuukokudouzoinoo-toresutorannitouchakushita.yokohabanohiroitatemonode,misenourakarakigayaneniooikabusaruyounihaeteita.kanban,yane,gaiheki,iroaseteinaibashowosagasuhougamuzukashiikuraida.tennnainiwajuudaihodonojidouhanbaikigaichiretsuninarabi,sonoshoumenni,hitoajitougarashiyahaizaranookaretahosoite-burugafutatsusetchisareteita.sumininarabujuunenijoumaenoa-ke-dokatamitainobi-ji-emuwa,sabiretatennnainofunnikiwohonnnosukoshidakeakarukushitekureteita.sanhyakuenwomenruijihankinitounyuushi,chourigakanryousurumadetabakowosuttematta.wamaruisunisuwari,hitotsudaketenmetsushiteirukeikoutouwomiageteita.konoonnnanokowa,orenokanshiwoshiteiruma,douyatteshokujiwotorutsumorinanodarou?nomazukuwazutoiuwakedewanaidarouga,souiwaretemonattokudekirudakenobukimisagakanojoniwaatta.amarinikikaijimiteiru,todemoiuka.ningenmiganainoda.atsuibakarideyasuppoiajinosurutenpurasobawotairagetanochiwa,inryoujihankideko-hi-wokattenonda.amattaruiaisuko-hi-wa,kawaitashintainishimiwatatteitta.yomeisankagetsuwokitteokinagara,wazawazajihankinomazuimeshiwotabenikitanowa,oregasoreshikashiranakattakarada.sakkimadenooreniwa,somosomo,toudeshite,koukyuunamisedeshokujiwotorutoiusentakushigasonzaishinakatta.kokosuunennobinbouseikatsude,orewasouzouryokutoiumonowoarakataushinatteshimattamitaidatta.shokujiwooeteapa-tonimodottaorewa,bo-rupenwonigiri,techouwohiraki,sokoniaratametekongonohoushinwokajougakikisurukotonishita.hajimewa,yaritaikotowokangaeruyoriyaritakunaikotowokangaeruhougarakudattaga,tewougokashiteirutoshidaini,shinumaeniyatteokitaikotomoatamaniukabuyouninattekita.shinumaeniyaritaikotodaigakuniikanaihatarakanaiyokubounisakarawanaioishiimonowotaberukireinamonowomiruishowokakuNarusetoattehanashiwosurutoatteomoiwouchiakerusore,yameteoitahougaiidesuyofurimukuto,heyanosuminisuwatteitahazunoga,itsunomanikahaigonitatte,orenotemotowonozokikondeita.kanojogayubisashitanowa,yorinimoyotte,toatteomoiwouchiakerutokakaretakudaridatta.kanshiinttenowa,kouiutokoromadenozoite,kuchidashisurugimugaarunoka?toorewakiita.wasonoshitsumonniwakotaenakatta.kawarini,orenikoutsugeta.sonosandesuga,iroiroarimashite,juunanasaideshussanshiteirundesu.sonomamakoukouwotaigaku,juuhachisaidekekkonshimasuga,ichinengoniwarikon,nijuusainogenzaiwajikkadekosodatewoshiteimasu.ninengo,kanojowatobiorijisatsusurukotoninatteimasu.insannnaishowonokoshite.aaimaainiittemo,rokunakotoninarimasenyo.soreni,san,anatanokotonantehotondooboetemasenkara.mochiron,juusainotokinikawashita,reinoyakusokunokotomonodokaraumakukoegadetekonakatta.hainonakanokuukiga,isshundeusumattakigashita.aasokomade,orenojijounikuwashiinokayattonokotodeikiwohakidashi,douyouwohisshinioshikakushinagara,orewakiita.sonokuchiburikarasuruto,antawa,korekarasakiniokorukotosubetegawakatterunoka?wani,sandomewomabatakasetanochi,kubiwoyokonifutta.watashigashitteirunowa,kongo,sannojinseitosonoshuuhendeokorukamoshirenakattakotodesu.mottomo,imatonattewaiminonaijouhoudesukedone.jumyouwouttakotoniyotte,anatanomiraiwaoukikukawatteshimaimashitakara.soreni,watashigashitteirunowa,sonookorukamoshirenakattakotononakademo,tokunijuuyounakotogaradakedesuwatechouwonozokikondamama,migitewoyukkuriagete,kamiwomiminikakeru.anatanitottesanwa,totemojuuyounasonzaidattayoudesune.sannojinseinoarasujiniwa,sannokotobakarikaitearimashitasorewaakumadesoutaitekinahanashidatoorewatsuihiteishita.tanokotoga,orenitottewajuuyoujanasasugitattedakedarousoukamoshiremasennetowaitta.tonikaku,watashiniierukotowa,imakarasanniainiikukotowa,jikannorouhidatoiukotodesu.omoidewodainashinisarerudakedesuyookizukaiarigatou.shikashi,tokkunidainashidademo,jikannosetsuyakuniwanattadeshou?kamoshirenaina.shikashi,anta,sonnnakantanni,mirainokotowohonnninnihanashitemoiimononanoka?wakubiwokashigeru.gyakunishitsumonsasetemoraimasukedo,nazehanashitewaikenaitoomottandesuka?souiwaretemiruto,nanimoomoitsukenakatta.karinioregamirainojouhouworiyoushitenanikaakujiwohatarakoutoshitemo,sonotokiwakarahonbunirenrakugaiki,orenojumyougakirerudakeda.watashitachiwa,kihontekiniwa,anatagaheionnnayoseiwookurukotowonozondeimasutowaitta.sonotamenikoushite,anatanomirainimotozuitajogenwoshitari,keikokuwoshitaritoittakotomosurundesuorewaatamawokaita.konoonnnanokoninanikaiikaeshiteyaritakunatta.naa,antawaima,oregakizutsuitarishitsuboushitarisurukotowomizennifuseidakininatteirunokamoshirenai.dagasonokouiwa,kizutsuitarishitsuboushitarisurujiyuuwoorekaraubattatomoierunjanainoka?souaatatoeba,oregakarini,antanokuchikarakansetsutekinidewanakute,nokuchikarachokusetsunisonojijitsuwokiitekizutsukeraretakattatoomotteitatoshitara,antanoshitakotowaosekkaidawamendoukusasounitameikiwotsuita.soudesuka.watashitoshitewazenninotsumoridattandesukedone.karinisoudattatoshitara,shoushoukaruhazuminahatsugendattakamoshiremasen.moushiwakearimasensouiuto,assariatamawosageta.aatada,hitotsudake,itteokimasu.korekaraokorudekigotonitaishite,amari,kouseisatokaseigouseitokawokitaishinaihougaiidesuyo.anatawajumyouwoutteshimattandesu.sorewa,konomattakurikutsunokayotteinaifujourinashikuminosekaini,mizukaratobikondeshimattakotowoimishimasu.sokodejiyuuyakenrinankanitsuiteshuchoushitemo,hotondomudadesuyo.anatawajibundetobikondandesukarasouiuto,waheyanosuminimodotte,futatabisankakusuwariwoshita.towaie,sukunakutomokonkaiwa,anatanokizutsuitarishitsuboushitarisurujiyuutoyarawosonchoushite,anatagasonorisutonikaitahokanokoumokunitsuitewa,kuchidashiwoshinaideokoutoomoimasu.douzowosukini,taninnimeiwakuwokakenaihannide,yaritaikotowoyattekudasai.watashiwatomemasenkaraiwarenakutattesoushiteyarusa,toorewaomou.konotokigakokoronashikakanashisounakaowoshitanoo,orewaminogashitewainakatta.shikashi,sonohyoujougaimisurutokoromadewa,fukakukangaetemiyoutowashinakatta.

4.kotaeawasetoikimashou

kokokaraorenomanukeburiwakasokusuru.orewanidenwawokakerudakeda,sugumodorutoitte,wazawazaapa-tonosotonideta.kanojonitsuuwanaiyouwokikaretakunakutesoushitatsumoridattanodaga,annnojou,wachokochokoushirowotsuitekita.jibunkaradarekanidenwawokakerunowahisashiburidatta.orewakeitainogamennihyoujisareteiru,Wakanatoiumojiwonagaimamitsumeteita.apa-tonouranohayashidewa,natsuchuugakorokorotonaiteita.douyaraorewa,takagadenwanikinchoushiteirurashikatta.omoeba,kodomonokorokarazutto,jibunkaradarekawoasobinisasotari,kaiwawomotometaritoittakotowoshinaidekita.soreniyottetakusannokanouseiwoushinattanomojijitsudaga,onajikurainowazurawashisakaranogareraretanomojijitsuda.tokunikoukaimomanzokumonai.shikouwoittanuchikiru.chokugoniotozurerusuubyoukannoshikouteishiworiyoushite,keitainotsuuwabotanwoosu.denwasaekaketeshimaebakotchinomonoda.shaberunaiyouwa,doutodemonarudarou.Ko-Ruotogakinchouwotakameru.ichikai,nikai,sankai.orewakonotokininatte,youyakutsuuwaaitegadenwanidenaikanouseigaarukotowoomoidasu.nagaimakouiukotowoshitekonakattakara,atamanodokokade,denwawokakerebaaitewaitsudemodetekurerumonodatoomoikondeitayouda.yonkai,gokai,rokukai.douyaraimasugudenwaniderareruyounajoukyoudewanairashii.kokoronodokokadeandoshiteirujibungairu.Ko-Ruotogahachikainitasshitatokorode,akirametetsuuwashuuryoubotanwooshita.denwawokaketaaite,wakanawadaigakunokouhainoonnnanokoda.shokujinidemosasoutsumoridatta.soshitemoshikotogaumakuhakobuyoudeareba,orenojumyougatsukirumade,zuttohataniitemoraitakatta.kokonikite,totsuzen,sabishisagakomiagetekitanoda.jinseinoowarigameikakuninatte,massakinikanjitahenkawa,koremadenooredewakangaerarenaihodonohitokoishisadatta.tonikakumouretsunidarekatohanashigashitakunatta.wakanawa,daigakudeyuiitsuorenikouiwomuketekureteitaningenda.kotoshinoharu,madanyuugakushitatedattawakanawa,reinofuruhonnyadeoretodeatta.boroboronokabikusaihonwokuiiruyounimitsumeruwakanani,orewajamada,hayakusokowodoketoiushisenwookutteitanodaga,kanojowasonoshisenwokyokkaishite,hyottoshitara,watashinirokotsunashisenwookurukarewa,mioboewanaimonono,itsukadokokadeshiriattanakananodewa?toiushinnnyuuseiniarigachinakanchigaiwookoshita.ano,moshikashite,dokokadewoaishimashita?towakanawaoreniosoruosorukiita.iyatoorewahiteishita.kokodeaunogahajimetedaare,soudesuka.shitsureishimashitawakanawajibunnokanchigainikizuitarashiku,kimazusounakaodemewosorashita.ga,sugunikiwotorinaoshitayounabiemiwoukabe,kouitta.jaa,tsumari,watashitachiwa,konokoshotendedeattandesune?kondowaoregakonwakusurubandatta.souiukotoninarundatoomousouiukotoninarundesuyo.sutekidesunetowakanawaii,koshowohondananimodoshita.suunichigo,oretachiwadaigakudesaikaisurukototonatta.soreirai,nandokachuushokuwotomonishi,sonotabinikougisotchinokedehonyaongakunitsuitenaganagatokatariatta.jibunyorihonwoyonderudousedaijinnideattanowahajimetedesutowakanawamewokagayakaseteitta.tadayonderudakedayo.sokokaraorewa,nanimoeteinaitoorewakotaeta.sonohonnohonrainokachiwohikidasutamenoukezaraga,oreniwanainda.yatterukotowa,nabekarakozaranitairyounosu-puwonagashikomunihitoshii.iretahatakaraafuredashite,sapparimininaranaisouiumononandesukane?towakanawakubiwokashigeru.tatoemininaranaiyounimietemo,suguniwasureruyounimietemo,ichidoyondamonowazettaininounodokokaninokotteite,honnninmokizukanaitokorodeyakunitatteirumonodatowatashiwaomotterundesukedosouiukotomoarukamoshirenaina.tada,sukunakutomoorewajibungasoudakarakosoiundagawakamononouchinidokushozukeninarunante,fukenkounakotodatoomou.dokushonante,tanisurukotononainingengayarukotosasan,yarukotoganaindesuka?arubaitoigaiwa,tokuninainatooregakotaeruto,wakanawatsutsumikakusanaiegaowoukabe,kondo,fuyashiteagemasuyo.yarukototoitteorenokatawokozuita.sorekaraorenokeitaiwokattenihiroiagete,jibunnoadoresutobangouwotourokushita.anotoki,gasudenininshin,kekkon,shussan,rikonwooe,orenokotonadowasureteshimatteirutoiukotowoshitteitara,orewaWakananitaishitemottoiromewotsukatteitanodarou.shikashiharugoronoorewa,aikawarazutonoyakusokuwotaisetsunishiteite,nijuusaimadezettainiurenokotteyaroutokatakukesshinshiteita.dakarajibunkarawakananirenrakusurukotowanakattashi,mukoukarame-ruyadenwagakitemo,ni,santsuukasuufundekiriageruyounishiteita.amarikitaisasetewaikenai,toomotteita.itsudatteorewa,sukuigatakumanowaruiningendattatoiukotoda.rusudenwonokosukiniwanarenakatta.denwawokaketamunewotsutaeyouto,orewawakananime-ruwookutta.totsuzendewaruikedo,ashita,dokokaikanaika.motokinakunarisuginaiyou,keredomowakananonakaniaruoretoiuningennoinshouwokyokutanniwakowasanaiyou,shinchounibunshouwoneriage,soushinshita.henjiwasugunikita.sonokotoninagusameraretanowamachigainakatta.orenokotowokinikaketekureteiruningengamadairunoda.henimonaku,kochiramosugunihenjiwookutteyarou,toomottayasakini,orewajibunnokanchigainikizuita.todoitame-ruwa,wakananomonodewanakatta.soredakenara,madayokatta.shikashi,temotonokeitainogamennihyoujisareteiruEimojiretsugaimishiteirunowa,jushinshanofuzaidatta.tsumari,kouiukotoda.wakanawame-ruadoresuwohenkoushite,keredomo,sorewoorenishirasenakatta.oretorenrakukanounajoutaiwoijisuruhitsuyouwanai,tohandanshitatoiukotoda.mochiron,sorewa,kanojonotechigaidatoiukanouseimoatta.imakarasugunidemo,kanojokaraadoresuhenkounotsuuchigakurutoiukanouseimoatta.shikashioreniwa,nantonaku,kakushingaatta.kigenwatokkunisugiteitanoda.utsuronamedekeitainogamenwomitsumeruorenoyousuwomite,wajijouwosasshitarashii.tsukatsukatoayumiyottekite,orenotemotowonozokikonda.sate,kotaeawasetoikimashoutowaitta.anatagakondenwawokaketaonnnanokowa,anatanitotte,saigonokiboudeshita.Wakanasanwa,anatawoaishitekuretakamoshirenakatta,saigonohitodesu.kanojogaanataniapuro-chishitekiteitaHarunokanni,anatanohoukarakanojonihatarakikaketeireba,imagoroanatatachiwa,kinoaukoibitotoshitenakayokuyatteitatoomoimasu.sounatteireba,jumyounokachigakonnnaniochirukotomonakattadeshou.aademo,chotto,osokattadesune.Wakanasanwamou,anatanokotonante,doudemoyokunatteimasu.ie,soredokoroka,jibunnokouinikotaetekurenakattasannokotowosukunakarazuurandeite,saikindekitakoibitoo,anatanimisetsuketeyaritaitokangaeteirukuraidesumenomaeniiruningennitsuitekatatteirutowaomoenaihodotsukihanashitakuchoude,waiu.igo,anatawosukininaroutoshitekureruhitowa,nidotoarawaremasen.anatagataninnokotoo,jibunnosabishisawoumerudougukurainishikamiteinaitoiukotowa,angaiminukareteshimaumononandesuyotonariheyanomadokarawa,tanoshigenakoegakikoeta.daigakuseinodanjosuuningasawaideirurashikatta.madokaramoreruakariwa,orenoheyakaramoreruakaritowakurabemononinaranaikuraiakarukumieta.izennoorenara,amarikinishinaidearoukoukeidattaga,imanooreniwa,sasarukoukeidatta.saiakunotaimingudekeitaiganatta.wakanakaranoridaiyarudatta.mushishiteshimaoutomokangaetaga,gonimatakakattekitaramendounanode,orewadenwanideta.san,sakkidenwakaketekimashitayone?doukashitandesuka?osorakuitsumotokawaranaikuchoudesouittanodarouga,sakihodonohanashinoseika,wakananokoegaorewosemeteiruyounikikoeta.imasaradenwanantekaketekitedouiutsumoridesuka?todemoiwareteiruyouna.warukattana,machigaetekakechimattandaorewatsutometeakaruku,souitta.soudesuka.maa,soudesuyone.san,jibunkarahitonidenwakakeruyounahitojaarimasenmonnetowakanawawaratta.sonowaraikatanimomata,azakerigakomerareteiruyounikanjirareta.dakarakoso,watashiwaanatawomikagittandesuyotoiwareteirukigashita.aa,soudanawazawazakakenaoshitekuretearigatou,toitteorewatsuuwawokitta.tonariheyawa,issounigiyakaninatteita.heyanimodorukininarezu,orewasonobadetabakonihiwotsuketa.nihonsuioeruto,kinjonosu-pa-ma-kettonimukai,yukkuritotennnaiwomawatte,bi-runorokukanpakkutotouage,kappura-menwokaimonoKagoniireta.sokodeorewahajimete,jumyouwoutteetasanjuumanennitewotsukerukotoninatta.sekkakudakarazeitakuwoshiteyaroutoomottewaitanodaga,naniwokaebazeitakuniatarunoka,oreniwasappariwakaranakatta.watenimottaKagoni,karori-meitoyamineraruuo-ta-toittaajikenaiinshokubutsuwotairyouniireteita.kanojogasouittakaimonowosurukotojitaiwamattakufushigidewanainodaga,kounyuushitasorerawokanojogajissainikuchinisurubamenwosouzoushiyoutoshitemo,umakudekinakatta.dokokaningenminokanjirarenaikonanode,shokujitoiumottomogenshitekideningentekinakouiganiawanainoda.sorenishitemoaakorejaamarude,doukyochuunokoibitodoushiganinindekaimonowoshiteirumitaidana,toorewakokorononakadekossoritsubuyaita.sorewajitsunibakagetakeredomoshiawasenasakkakudatta.surechigauhitobitogaoretoonajisakkakuwodaiteitekurerebaii,tosaeomotta.nennotameniitteokuto,orewakonotoiuonnnanokonosonzaijitaiwa,zuttoutomashikukanjiteiru.tada,mukashikaraorewa,doukyoshiteiruonnnanokotoheyaginomamadekaketeshokuzaiyasakewokattekaettekurutoiukouini,hisokaniakogarewodaiteita.souiukotowoshiteirurenchuuwomikakerutabini,asaitameikigamoretamonodatta.souiuwakede,tatoekanshigamokutekidarouto,wakaionnnanokotoyachuunosu-pa-dekaimonowosurunowatanoshikatta.munashiishiawase.demohontounisoukanjirunodakara,shikataganai.wahitoashisakiniserufurejidetebayakukaikeiwosumaseteita.kaimonobukurowoburasagete,ninindeapa-tonimodotta.tonariheyanosawagiwaaikawarazutsuzuiteite,kabenomukoukarahinpanniashiotogakikoeta.shoujikiitte,orewakareragaurayamashikatta.koremade,konnnakimochininattakotowanakatta.tanoshigenisawaideirurenchuuwomitemo,ittainanigasonnnanitanoshiindarou?kurainokansoushikaidakanakatta.daga,shiwoishikisuruyouninattakotoniyotte,koremadeoregahisshiniyugametekitakachikanwamigotoniseijoukasareteshimattayouda.hitonamini,hitokoishikatta.kouiutoki,taiteinoningenwa,kazokutoiusonzainisukuiwomiidasoutosurunokamoshirenaina,toorewaomotta.donnnajoukyouninaroutokazokudakewamikatadeitekurerunodakara,saishuutekiniwasokonikaerubekinandasouiukangaekatagaarukotowa,shitteiru.shikashi,kazokutoiumonogadarenitottemokokoroatatamarusonzaidearutowakagiranai.sukunakutomoorewa,nokorisankagetsu,nanigaattemo,kazokutodakewarenrakuwotoranaitsumorideita.yomeiganokorisukunaikarakoso,mizukarafukainaomoiwoshiniikukotodakewa,zettainisakenakerebanaranakatta.osanaikorokara,orewaotoutoniryoushinnoaijouwoubawaretsuzuketekita.motomoto,otoutonohouga,arayurunouryokumendeoreyorisugureteita.seikakumomassugudattashi,semotakaku,kaomoyokatta.juunisainokorokarajuukyuusainoimamadekoibitowotayashitakotowanakattashi,toutteirudaigakumooreyoriyuushuudatta.undoushinkeimoyoku,koukouseinotokiniwaKoushi 5.korekaraokorukotosubete

akariwokeshitesakewonomitsuzuketa.saiwainakotoni,konohinoorewayasurakaniyoukotoniseikoushiteita.kouiutokiwakibunnonagarenisakarawazu,mushiromizukarazetsubounofuchinitobikondenamaatatakaijikorenbinnihitarukotokosogatettoribayakutachinaorukotsunanoda.minaretaheyaga,sukoshidakechigauimiwomochihajimeteita.madokarasashikomutsukiakaridekonnironisomari,natsunoyorufuugafukikomusonoheyawa,sumidezashikiwarabemitainijittoshiteirunosonzaimoatte,marudeimamadetowaishitsunakuukannikanjirareta.orewakonoheyani,souiukaogaarukotowoshiranakatta.jibungabutaisodeniiruyounakankakugaatta.sokokarafumidashitatoki,youyakuorenoengigahajimaruyounakigashita.totsuzen,imanojibunninara,nanidattedekirukigashitekita.sorewayopparattakotodeichijitekinijibunnomunouwowasuretatamenogoumannisuginainodaga,orewajibunnonakadenanikagakawaritsutsuarunodatokanchigaishitanoda.nimukatte,takarakanisengensuru.orewa,nokosaretasankagetsunomani,jumyouwoutteetakonosanjuumanende,nanikawokaetemiserusouiuto,kanninokotteitabi-ruwonomihoshite,te-burunoueniikioiyokuoita.shikashi,nohannnouwahiyayakanamonodatta.suusenchimesenwoagete,soudesukatodakeitte,matano-tonimesenwootoshita.orewakamawazutsuzuketa.tattasanjuumanendarouto,korewaorenoinochida.sansenmanyasanjuuokuyorimokachinoarusanjuumannishiteyaru.shinimonoguruidedoryokushite,konosekainiisshimukuiteyaruyopparattaorenoatamaniwa,sorewatotemoiidaishinikikoeta.soredemo,washirakeppanashidatta.mina,onajiyounakotowoiundesuyopenwowakiniokuto,wahizawokakae,maniagowoumeteitta.nitayounadaishio,koremadegokaikuraikikimashita.mina,shikigachikazukunitsure,hassougadondonkyokutanninatteikundesuyo.tokuni,amarimitasareteitatowaienaijinseiwookuttekitahitowa,sonokeikougatsuyoindesu.kakegotonimaketsuzuketekitahitoga,yorihigenjitsutekinaichihatsugyakutenbakariwonerauyouninarunotoonajirikutsude,jinseinimaketsuzuketekitahitowa,higenjitsutekinashiawasewonozomuyouninarundeshoune.oukunohitoga,shiwomaenishitesoutaikasaretanamanokagayakiwomanoatarinishite,youyakukatsuryokurashiimonowotorimodoshi,koremadenojibunwadoushiyoumonainingendattaga,ayamachinikizuitaimanojibunninara,nanidattedekirutoiushikouniochiitteshimaundesugaomouni,soushitahitotachiwachimeitekinakanchigaiwookashiteshimatteimasu.karerawa,youyakusuta-tochitennitattatoiudakenandesu.maketsuzukenogyanburude,youyakureiseisawotorimodoshitatoiudakenandesu.sorewoichihatsugyakutennochansudatokanchigaisuruto,rokunakotoninarimasenyo.aasan,yokukangaetemitekudasai.anatanojumyounokachigaasokomadehikukattanowa,anataganokorinosanjuunende,nanihitotsunashitogerarenaikaradesu.sorewawakatteirundeshou?watsukihanasuyouni,itta.sanjuunendenanihitotsunashitogerarenaiyounahitoga,tattasankagetsudenaniwokaerarerutteiundesuka?aayatteminakya,wakaranaisabaataritekinihanronshitaoredattaga,sonokotobanoamarinokuukyosani,jibundemounzarishita.yarumaekaratokkuniwakarikitteirunoda.kanojonoiibunwa,dokomademotadashii.motto,arikitarideheibonnnamanzokuwomotomeruhougakenmeidatoomoimasuyotowaitta.dousemou,torikaeshiwatsukanaindesu.sankagetsutoiukikanwa,nanikawokaeruniwamijikasugimasu.towaie,nanimoshinaidesugosuniwashoushounagasugimasu.dattara,chiisakutemokakujitsunashiawasewotsumikasaneteittahouga,rikoudatowaomoimasenka?katounanteomoukaramakerundesuyo.makenonakanikachiwomiidasuikikatanohouga,shitsubouwasukunakutesumimasuwakattawakatta,antanoiukotowatadashii.dagaseironwamoutakusandatoorewakubiwoyokonifutta.yopparatteinakerebamukininattehanronwotsuzuketeitakamoshirenaiga,imanooreniwakanojonoseironwokutsugaesudakenokiryokuwanokotteinakatta.kittoorewa,jibunnomunousatteyatsuo,imaichirikaishikireteinaindarou.aanaa,oshietekurenaika,korekaraokorukoto,subete.orewasonoushinawaretasanjuunenkano,dousugosukotoninatteitanda?sorewokikeba,mou,jibunnikajounakitaiwoidakanakutesumuyouninarukamoshirenaiwashibarakukuchiwohirakanakattaga,futoakirametayouniitta.soudesune.konosaianatawa,subeteshittahougaiinokamoshiremasen.aatada,nennotameniitteokimasukedo,watashinohanashiwokiite,anatagajiboujikininaruhitsuyouwaarimasenkarane.watashigashitteirunowa,okorukamoshirenakattakedo,imadewamou,zettainiokorienaikotonandesukarawakatteru.oregakorekarakikunowa,uranaimitainamonosa.aasoshitehitotsuiwasetemorauto,jiboujikininaruhitsuyounantenowa,itsudattenainda.tadasounaruhokanaikarasounarutoiudakedesounaranaikotowonegaimasuyotowaitta.jihibikinoyounaotogashita.kyodainatougataoretayounaotodatta.soregahanabinootodatokizukumadenijikangakakattanowa,oregakokosuunen,matomoniuchiagehanabitoiumonowomiteinakattakarada.itsudattesorewa,madogoshinimirumonodatta.yataidekattaokonomiyakiwotabenagaramiruyounamonodewanakattashi,tewonigiriainagarakoibitonokaotokougonimirumonodemonakatta.busshintsuitatokikara,hikagemononoorewa,hitonoatsumarubashowosaketeikitekita.jibungasouiubashoniirunowamachigattakotonoyounikanjiraretashi,sokodedarekashiriainiattatokinokotowokangaeruto,koshigahiketa.shougakuseinokorowa,darekanishiiraredemoshinaikagiri,kouennimopu-runimogakkounourayamanimoshoutengainimoNatsumatsurinimohanabitaikainimoikanaiyounishiteita.koukouseininattemosakaribaniwachikazukazu,machiwoarukutokiwadekirudakeoudouriwosaketa.saigoniuchiagehanabiwomitanowa,hontouniosanaikoroda.sonotokimotonariniwa,gaitakigasuru.majikademiruuchiagehanabigadorehodooukiika,orewamouwasureteshimatteita.majikadekikusonootogadorehodooukiikamo,douyounioboeteinakatta.chikakudewakayakunonioigasurunodarouka?kemuriwadonoteidosoraninokorunodarouka?kaijounohitobitowadonnnakaodehanabiwonagamerunodarouka?souyattehitotsuhitotsukangaetemiruto,orewahanabinitsuitehotondonanimoshiranakatta.madonosotowonagametaitoiuyuuwakugaorewoosottaga,gamiteirutemae,souiuwabishiimanewosurukiniwanarenakatta.sonnnakotowoshitara,nikonnnakazeniiwarerukamoshirenai.sonnnanihanabigamitainara,miniikebaiinjanaidesuka?.soushitaraorewanantokotaerudarou?mawarinomewokinishitekiokureshiteshimaukaraiyada,todemokotaerunoka?doushiteorewayomeimonokorisukunainoni,imadanitaninnomegakininatteshimaunodarou?hisshiniyuuwakutotatakauorewoazawaraukanoyouni,waorenomaewoyokogiri,amidowoake,madokaramiwonoridashiteuchiagehanabiwonagamehajimeta.kireinamonowomitekandoushiteirutoiuyoriwa,mezurashiimonowomitekanshinshiteirutoiuyousudattaga,naniniseyo,souiumononikyoumiganaiwakedewanairashii.oioi,sonnnamonomiteteiinoka,kanshiinsan.oregatotsuzennigedashitarishitaradousurutsumorida?wahanabiwomitsumetamama,mihatteitehoshiindesuka?tohinikuppokuitta.masaka.hayaitokoroinakunattehoshiine.antanimirareteruto,doumoyarinikuisoudesuka.yohodoushirometaikotodemoarundesukane.aachinamini,anataganigedashite,watashitoitteikyoriijouhanareteshimattabaai,yaharitashanimeiwakuwokakeruishigaarumonotominasare,jumyouwonukareteshinukotoninarimasunode,okiwotsukekudasaiitteikyoritte,dorekuraida?sokomadegenmitsunamonodewaarimasenkedo,daitai,hyakume-torutoiutokorodewanaideshoukasouiukotowasaishoniittehoshiimonoda.kiwotsukeruyotoorewaitta.tsugitsugitokokimiyoiotogasoranihibiita.uchiagehanabiwakakyounihaittayoudatta.itsunomanika,tonariheyanosawagiwaosamatteita.kareramokonohanabiwominiittanokamoshirenai.soushiteyouyaku,wahanashihajimeta.okorukamoshirenakattakotonitsuite.sate,ushinawaretasanjuunenkannokotodesugaaamazu,anatanodaigakuseikatsuwa,mabatakumaniowarimasutowaitta.seikatsuhiwokasegi,honwoyomi,ongakuwokiki,atowahitasuranemurudake.kawaribaenonaikarapponamainichiwa,dandanto,ichinichiichinichiwokubetsusurukotosaekonnnannisaseteikimasu.sounatteshimauto,hibiwa,tobuyounihayakusugirumonodesu.nanihitotsutashikanamonowaminitsukerarenaimamadaigakuwosotsugyoushiteshimattaanatawa,hinikunimo,kibounimichiafureteitakoronojibungamottomokeibetsushiteitashokunitsukimasu.sokodeisagiyokujoukyouwoukeirerarerebayokattanodesuga,anatawadoushitemokatsutetokubetsudeattajibunwowasurerukotogadekizu,kokowaorenohontounoibashojanaitoiuishikigajamawoshite,doushitemoshokubaninajimemasen.mainichi,shindamedejitakutoshokubawooufukushi,miwokonanishitehataraite,monowokangaeruhimamonaku,shidaini,wosakewonomukotobakarigatanoshimininatteikimasu.itsukawaerakunatteyarutoiuyashinmokie,kodomonokoroniegaitarisoutowakakehanaretaningenninarundesukesshitemezurashiihanashijanaitoorewakuchiwohasanda.sou,kesshitemezurashiihanashijaarimasen.sokoniarunowa,itatteheibonnnazetsuboudesu.mottomo,sokokarauketorukutsuuwahitosorezoredesu.anatanitotte,anatajishinwa,dareyorimoyuushuudeiruhitsuyougaarujinbutsudeshita.seishintekinitayorubekiaitegainaianatanosekaiwa,anatagaichinindesasaerushikanakattandesu.sonoichihonbashiragaoretatokinishoujitakutsuuwa,anatawohametsunimukawaserunijuubunnnamonodeshitahametsu?toorewakikikaeshita.kizukebaanatawa,sanjuudaikouhannisashikakatteimashita.kodokunaanatanoshumiwa,baikuninotteatemonakuhashirukotodeshita.shikashi,anatamoshittenotouri,sorewakikennnanorimonodesu.tokuni,nakabajibunnojinseiwoakirameteshimatteiruhitowonoseteiruyounabaainiwa.aafukouchuunosaiwaiwa,anatagadarekanountensurukurumatoshoutotsushitari,hokoushawohanetarishitawakedewanaku,tannniichinindetentoushitadakedatta,toiutendesu.shikashisonojikoniyotte,anatawaushinaimashita.kaonohanbunto,arukukinouto,yubinotaihanokaonohanbunwoushinau,toiukotobanoimiworikaisurunowakantandattaga,souzousurunowamuzukashikatta.tabunsorewa,daregamitemo,kaodattabashotoshikaninshikidekinaiyouna,santantaruarisamaninarutoiukotodarou.jishinnoyoushiwoyoridokoronohitotsutoshiteitaanatawa,iyoiyosaigonoshudanniderukotowokangaemasu.desuga,doushitemoatoichihogafumikiremasendeshita.saigoninokottaittekinokibouga,sutekirenakattandesu.soredemo,itsukaiikotogaarukamoshirenaitoiukibougaaatashikanisorewa,darenimohiteidekinaihanashinandesuga,demo,soredakedesu.arutanenoakumanoshoumeinisugimasen.sonnnatayorinaikibouwomuneni,anatawagojuusaimadeikitsuzukemasugakekkyoku,nanihitotsuerarenaimama,boroboroninatte,ichinindeshindeikimasu.darenimoaisarezu,darenimokiokusarezu.saigomade,konnnahazujanakattandatonagekinagarakimyounamonoda.sonohanashio,orewa,sunnnaritoukeirerukotogadekiteshimatta.sate,gokansouwa?soudana.hitomazu,sanjuunenuriharatteoite,hontouniyokattatoomotteruyosouorewakotaeta.tsuyogaridewanakatta.honnninmoitteitayouni,noiuokorukamoshirenakattakotowa,gyakuniimatonattewa,zettainiokorienaikotonanoda.dousenara,sankagetsumonokosanaide,sannichidakenokoshiteuriharaebayokattanaimakarademomaniaimasukedonetogaitta.madaanatawa,nikai,jumyounobaibaigayurusareteimasukaranokorisannichininareba,antamoorenohatakarainakunarundarou?ee.doushitemowatashinosonzaigakinikuwanaitoiunara,sousurukotomosentakushinohitotsudesuyooboetokuyotoorewaitta.jissainotokoro,nokorinosankagetsunimokoretoittakibounomotenaiorenitottewa,sannichidakenokoshitejumyouwouriharaunogamottomosaetayarikatananodarou.shikashi,sorewoomoitodomaraserunowa,yaharikokonikitemo,soredemo,itsukaiikotogaarukamoshirenaitoiuakumanoshoumeitekikibounanodatta.kokokaranosankagetsuwa,nohanashitaushinawaretasanjuunentowakanzennibetsumonoda.miraiwakakuteishiteinai.hyottoshitara,nanikaiikotogaarukamoshirenai.gamanshiteikitekiteyokattatoomoeruyounadekigotoga,konominiokirukamoshirenai.kanouseiwa,zerodewanai.soukangaeruto,madashinuwakeniwaikanakatta.mayonakaniamenootodemewosamashita.kowaretaamedoikarakoboretamizugajimenwotatakuotogataemanakukikoeteita.tokeiwomiruto,gozensanjisugiwosashiteita.amaikaorigaheyanitadayotteita.hisashikukaideinainioidattakara,soregaonnnamononoshanpu-nokaoridearutoiukotoniwanakakitsukenakatta.shoukyohoutekiniitte,sononioinoarujigadearukotowamachigainakatta.kangaerarerunowa,oreganeteirumanigafuronihaittatoiukotoda.shikashi,sonoketsuronwadoumoukeiregatakatta.jimandewanaiga,orenonemuriwaitsudatte,utatanetoyondeiikurainiasai.shinbunhaitatsuyauekainoashiototoitta,chottoshitamonootodesugunimewosamashiteshimau.sonnnaorega,gashawa-woabiteiruma,ichidomomewosamasanakattatoiunowamyoudatta.amenootoniumaikotomagireteitanodarouka.orewasonoketsuronwosakiokurinishita.shiriattabakarinoonnnanokogajibunnoiedeshawa-woabiteitatoomoutomyounakibunninattaga,sochiranitsuitemokangaenaikotonishita.soreyorimo,ashitanisonaetenemuruhitsuyougaatta.konnnaamenoyoruniokiteitatteshikataganai.shikashikantanninetsukesouniwanakatta.sokodeorewaitsumonoyouniongakunochikarawokarirukotonishita.urazunioitashi-ji-noichimai,Puri-Zumisuta-Rosutomanwomakuramotonopureiya-nisettoshite,heddohondekiitakorewaorenokattenarikutsudaga,nemurenuyoruniPuri-Zumisuta-Rosutomanwokikuyounayatsunimatomonajinseiwaokurenai.kouiuongakuwomochiite,orewasekaininajimezumatanajimoutoshinaijibunwoyurushisugita.sonotsukeo,ima,harawasareteirunokamoshirenai.

6.kawatteshimattahito,kawarnakattahito

amewayokuasamofuritsuzuiteita.kishougosugunikoudouniutsuranaikotonoiiwakeninarukurai,tsuyoiamedatta.okagedeorewa,korekarasubekikotonitsuitejikkurikangaerukotogadekita.shinumaeniyaritaikotorisutowooreganagameteiruto,gachikayottekite,kyouwadonnnakazenisugosundesuka?tokiitekita.kanojonokuchikarawaruinyu-suwokikasarerukotoninareteshimatteitaorewa,naniwoiwaretemodoujinaideirareruyoukakugowokimetetsuginokotobawomattaga,wasoredakeiuto,nochiwajittorisutowomiorosudakedatta.tokunifukaiiminonaishitsumondattarashii.orewasonnnao,aratametekansatsushita.hajimeteattatokikarazuttoomotteitakotodaga,nogaikenwa,sorenarinitotonotteiru.iya,hakkiriitteshimaou.youshinikagittahanashiwosureba,kanojowaorenokoumisonomonoda.suzushigename,yuuutsusounamayu,kitsukumusubaretakuchimoto,kireinakatachinoatama,yawarakasounakami,shinkeishitsusounayubi,hossoritoshitashiroifutomomoagehajimetarakiriganai.soredakeni,kanojogakonoheyawoarawaretasonoshunkankara,furumainiwakiwotsukauyouninatteita.amarinikonominigatchishitaonnnanokonomaedato,ukatsuniakubimodekinai.jibunnokuzuretahyoujouyamanukenaikizukaiwokakushitakunarunoda.moshikanshiinga,konoonnnanokototaishoutekina,minikukufutottafuketsunachuunennadodeareba,orewamottorirakkusushitejibunnoyaritaikotonitsuiteshoujikinikangaerukotogadekitadarou.shikashikoushitegahataniirukotode,orewajibunnoigandayokubouyanasakenaiganbounadowohitsuyouijounihajiruyouninatteshimatteita.korewakojintekinaikennandesukedotogaitta.sonorisutonikakareteirunowa,hontounianataga,kokoronosokokarayaritaitoomotteirukotonandesuka?oremosorenitsuitekangaetetatokonandakouittewanandesukedoaawatashiniwadoumo,anataga,jibundenaidarekaga,shinumaenishisounakotoworisutoninarabeteiruyounishikamienaindesuyosoukamoshirenainatoorewamitometa.hontounotokoro,oreniwashinumaeniyaritaikotonante,hitotsumonainokamoshirenai.shikashi,soredemonanimoshinaiwakeniwaikanaikara,kouyattedarekanomanewoshiterundasoredemo,mottoanatanimuitayarikatagaarukigasurundesukedonenaniyaraimifukanakotowoiuto,washoteinoichinimodotteitta.sonoasanioregatasshitaketsuronwa,tsuginoyounamonodatta.orewamousukoshi,jibunnoigandayokubouyanasakenaiganbounishoujikininaruhitsuyougaaru.mottozokuppoku,mottoatsukamashiku,mottogehinni,honnnounoomomukumamanisaigonosankagetsuwosugosubekinanoda.imasara,naniwotoritsukurouhitsuyougaarutoiunodarou?ushinaumononadonanimonaitowakatteiruhazunanoni.orewashinumaeniyaritaikotorisutowomouichidomitsume,iwokesshi,chijinnoichininnidenwawokaketa.kondonoaitewa,suuko-rudesorenioujitekureta.kasawomottesotonidetaoregaekinitsukukoroniwaamegayandeitanowa,oretoiuningennomanowarusawoshouchousurukanoyounadekigotodatta.sakkimadenoamegausonoyouniharewatattasoranoshitadekasawoteniaruiteiruto,jibunnomotteirumonogasuke-tokutsukananikanoyounifutekisetsunamononikanjirareta.nuretaromengagiragiratokagayaiteita.atsusakaranigeruyouniekinihaittaga,sokomosashitekawaranaiatsusadatta.resshaworiyousurunowahisashiburidatta.ho-munomachiaishitsunihairi,gomibakonoyokonisetchisaretajihankideko-rawokauto,benchinikoshiwooroshi,mitsukuchidenomihoshita.momineraruuo-ta-wokai,mewotojitekokukokutonondeita.madokarasoranoyousugamieta.sokoniwaussuratonijigaukandeita.sonnnagenshougaarukotosae,orewasukkariwasureteita.nijitoiugenshougadonoyounamonode,donoyounatokiniokori,donoyounainshouwohitonimotarasunokawashitteitahazunanodagamottomokisotekinachishiki,soregajitsuzaisurumonodearutoiukotoo,itsushikakanzenniwasureteshimatteitayoudatta.masaranamedesorewomite,hajimetekizukukotogaaru.soranikakarukyodainayumiwa,oreniwazenbudegoshikiteidonishikamiezu,nanaironiwanishokutarinai.aka,ki,midori,ao,murasaki.jibungatobashitanowananishokudarou,tosorezorenoirowokakuunoparettodemazetemite,soregadaidaitoaidattakotogawakatta.soudesune,yokumiteoitahougaiideshoutogayokodeitta.korega,saigonimirunijininarukamoshiremasenkarasoudanatoorewaunazuita.soshitesaranitsukekuwaeruto,konomachiaishitsuworiyousurukotodattenidotonaikamoshirenaishi,ko-rawonomunomokorekirikamoshirenaishi,akikanwonagerunomosaigoninarukamoshirenaiorewanomihoshitako-ranokanwomizuironogomibakonimukattehourinageta.kandoushigabutsukariauotogamachiaishitsunihibiita.nanidatte,saigoninarukamoshirenai.demosonnnano,jumyouwourumaekara,zuttosounandatowaiitsutsumo,nohatsugenwoukete,orewachottoaserihajimeteita.nijiyamachiaishitsuyako-rayaakikannitsuitewa,madaii.shikashikorekarashinumadenomani,orewaittai,atonanmainoshi-ji-wokikerudarou?nansatsunohonwoyomerudarou?nanhonnotabakowosuerudarou?souiukangaekatawoshidasuto,totanniorewasoraosoroshikunatta.shinutoiunowa,shinitsuzukeruigainokotosubete,nidotodekinakunarutoiukotonanoda.oritaekikarabasudejuugofunhodonotokoroniaruresutorande,orewanarusetoaukotoninatteita.narusewakoukoujidainoyuujindatta.sewaheikintoonajikasoreyorisukoshihikuiteido,shoushouhegafukasugirukaonomochinushidatta.atamanokaitengahayaku,hitowohikitsukeruyounashaberikatagadekirutameni,mawarikarasukareteita.sonnnakareto,hikagemononoorenonakagayokattatoiunowa,imaomoutofushiginahanashida.oretachiniwahitotsu,kyoutsuunokenkaigaatta.yonisonzaisurutaiteinomonogotoniwawaraitobasudakenoyochigaaru,toiunogasoreda.koukoujidai,yokuoretachiwafua-sutofu-dotenninagaikotoisuwatte,fukinshintoierukurainiaritoarayurunichijounodekigotowochakashitamonodatta.mataannnafuuni,subetewowaraitobashitakatta.soregahitotsumenomokutekidatta.soretodoujini,orewa,mouhitotsubetsunomokutekiwomottekareniainikiteita.narusenotouchakuwomatsuorenotonari,tsuurogawanosekiniwa,gasuwatteiru.yonninsekidaga,isugasorehodohirokutsukurareteinainode,oretonokyoriwashizentochikakunaru.sonnnashikinkyoride,waorewojittokanshishiteiru.tokidokioretomegaaukotogaattemo,mattakutonjakushinaiyousudeorewomitsumetsuzukeru.kouyatte,dokoniittemotsukimatottekiteshisenwookuritsuzuketekurutoorenokankeiseio,narusega,orenitottetsugounoiihoukounikanchigaisurebaiisoregaorenonozomidatta.sononozomigadoushiyoumonakunasakenaimonodearukotowa,oremomitomerutokoroda.shikashi,soushitainonara,sousuruhokaarumai.kanashiikotodaga,jumyouwouriharatteikouhajimete,oregahakkiritoyaritaitoomottakotogasoredattanodakara.naa,kanshiinsantoorewanihanashikakeru.nandeshoukaorewakubimotowokakinagaraiu,hitotsu,tanomigaarundagakorekarayattekuruotokoninaniwokikaretemotekitouninigoshitekure,toorewanitanomoutoshitanodaga,itsunomanikawheitoresugate-burunowakinitachi,manmennoemiwooretachinimuketeita.shitsureishimasu.gochuumonwaokimarideshouka?shikatanaku,orewako-hi-wochuumonshita.wheitoresugachuumonnokakuninwoshitekitanode,nennotameniorewanikiita.antawananimotanomanakuteiinoka?surutowa,myounikimazusounakaowoshita.aaano,hitomaede,watashinihanashikakenaihougaiidesuyonanikamazuikotodemoarunoka?ichiou,saishonimosetsumeishitatsumoridattandesukedoanodesune,watashitachikanshiinnosonzaitte,kanshitaishounohouigainiwachikakudekinaindesuyo.konoyounisouiutowawheitoresunosodewotsukami,chiisakuyusabutta.noiutouri,wheitoresuwa,naninohannnoumoshimesanakatta.watashigahitoniataerukankakuwa,subetenakattakototoshiteshorisarerundesutoitte,wagurasuwotenitoru.dakara,kouyattewatashigagurasuwomochiagetemo,kanojoniwagurasugauiteiruyounimieruwakedewaarimasen.dakaratoitte,gurasugakietayounimieruwakedemonaku,ugoiteinaiyounimieruwakedemonaku,tada,nakattakotonisaserarerundesu.watashitoiusonzaiwa,irukotowochikakusarenaidokoroka,inaikotosaechikakusarenaindesuyo.aatadashi,reigaigaarimasu.sorewa,yuiitsukanshiinnokotowochikakudekirusonzaidearu,kanshitaishoushagakarandabaaidesu.komattakotoni,anatanininshikisareteiruwatashisonomonowanakattakotonidekitemo,watashiwoninshikishiteiruanatadakewa,nakattakotonidekinaindesuyo.aayousuruni,san.anatawaima,daremoinaikuukannimukatteshaberikaketeiruyounimieteitandesuorewawheitoresunohyoujouwoukagau.kyoujindemomirukanoyounametsukide,kanojowaorenokotowomiteita.suufungo,orewatodoitako-hi-wosusurinagara,korewonomioetara,narusenimoawazunikaetteshimaoukatokangaeteita.karenotouchakugaatosuujuubyouosokereba,orewajissainisoushiteitadarou.dagakesshingakatamarusunzenni,narusegamisenihaittekurunogamieta.yamuwoezu,orewakarenimukattetemanekishita.sekinitsuitakarewa,ougesanioretonosaikaiwoyorokonda.yahari,orenotonariniiruniwamattakukizuiteinaiyousudatta.hisashiburidana.genkinishitetaka?tonarusewaitta.aa,soryamouatohantoshimoshinaiuchinishinuyatsunoiukotojanaina,toorewaomotta.tagainokinkyouwotsutaeaioerukoroniwa,oretachiwakoukoujidainimodottakanoyounachoushidehanaseruyouninatteita.gutaitekininaniwohanashitanokawaamarioboeteinaiga,kaiwanonakaminante,doudemoyokatta.jibuntachinobunpouotoushitemonogotowosabaiteikukotoga,oretachinokaiwanomokutekinanoda.narusetoorewa,hanashitahatakarawasureruyounakudaranaikotowotarenagashite,waraiatta.yomeinokennitsuitewa,issaihanasanaikotonishita.shinjitemoraerukadoukawakaranakattashi,sekkakunobawoshirakesasetakunakatta.oregaatohantoshimoshinaiuchinishinutoshittara,narusewaorenitaishitesukunakarazu,shitsureinonaiyounifurumaudarou.joudanwahodohodoniosaeteshimaudaroushi,nanikanagusametonarukotowoiwanakerebanaranaitoiukyouhakukannnennikararerudarou.souiukudaranaikotowokangaetehoshikunakatta.sonohitokotogakarenokuchikarahassarerumadewa,orewatanoshikuyareteitatoomou.tokorodetonarusewaomoidashitayouniitta.omae,mada,hewaegaiterunoka?iyatosokutoushitanochi,orewasorenitsuzukukotobawoshinchounisagashita.aadaigakunihaittekarawa,mattakuegakanakunattanayapparisoukatonarusewawaratta.madaegaitetara,doushiyoukatoomottayosorede,woowariidatta.jibundemookashinahanashidatowaomounodaga,konojuubyoutarazunoyaritoride,orenonakadesannenkaketetsuchikawaretekitanarusenitaisurukouiwa,jitsuniakkenaku,kieuseteshimatta.hontouniakkenaimonoda.nanikawotoritsukuroukanoyounikarukuchiwotobashitsuzukerukareni,orewakoeniwadasazuyobikakeru.naa,naruse.soredakewa,warachaikenakattanda.tashikaniorewa,sorewoakirameta.shikashi,dakaratoitte,sorewowaratteiiriyuuniwa,zettaininaranaindayo.omaenara,sorewowakattekureteirutoomottetandakedona.narusenimukeruorenoegaowa,dandantokatachidakenomononinatteitta.orewatabakonihiwotsuke,jibunkarawashaberazu,narusenokotobaniaizuchiwoutsudakeninatta.tonarinisuwatteitagaiu.aasate,kotaeawasetoikimashoukaorewakubiwochiisakuyokonifuttaga,wakamawazutsuzuketa.anatawaima,Narusesannokotogachoppirikiraininattadeshouga,miwoiutonarusesanmo,anatagaomotteiruhodoanatanokotowosuiteimasen.honraideareba,anatawaninengo,kyoutonitayounakatachidenarusesantoai,sasainakotowokikkakenikourontonari,kenkawakaresurukotoninatteimashita.aasounaranaiuchini,sousounikiriagetahougaiidesuyo.konohitonikitaishitemo,nanimoiikotowaarimasenkarasonotokioreganitaishitekanshakuwookoshitanowa,yuujinwobakanisaretakaradewanai.shiritakumonakattakotowoshirasaretakarademonaishi,hitsuyouijounihinikumeitahyougenwosurukotogakiniiranakattakarademonai.orenokatsutenoyumewoazawarattanarusehenoikariga,rifujinninimukeraretatoiuwakedemonai.dehananiniharawotatetanokatokikareruto,orewachottokomatteshimau.tonikakumasshoumendewanarusegapechakuchatonoutenkinakotowoshaberi,mayokodewagaguchiguchitokuraihanashiwoshi,sonohantaigawadewawakaionnnaniningakandakaikoedehobokantankotobanomideseiritsusurukaiwawokurihiroge,haigodewagekidanninrashikirenchuugajibunniyottayousudenesshinsounijironwokatari,okunosekidewagakuseishuudangatebyoushishinagaraougoedesawaideoritotsuzen,souiunogataerarenakunattanoda.uruseeyo,toorewaomotta.doushitemottoshizukanidekinainda?tsuginoshunkanniwa,orewatenonakanogurasuo,noirugawanokabeninagetsuketeita.souzouijounioukinaotogashitegarasugatobichittaga,soredemotennnaiwaisshunshizumarikaettadakede,matasugunisawagashikunatta.narusegamewomihiraiteorewomiteita.tenningakaketsuketekurunogamieta.gatameikiwotsuiteita.ittaiorewa,naniwoyatteirunodarou?senensatsuwonanmaikatoridashitete-buruniokuto,orewanigeruyounimisewodeta.basuninotteekihemodorutochuu,madonosotowonagameteiruto,furuboketabatthingusenta-gamenitsuita.orewakoushabotanwooshitebasuwoori,sokodesanhyakukyuuhodowoutta.battowookukoroniwa,tewashibiretechidarakede,omakeniasedakudatta.orewajihankidePokarisuettowokai,benchinikoshikaketeyukkurinominagara,kaishagaeritooboshikiotokotachigabattowofuruyousuwonagameta.shoumeinoguainoseikamoshirenaiga,samazamanamononoiroaiga,iyouniaoppokumieta.narusetoannnakatachidewakareteshimattakotoo,orewakoukaishiteinakatta.imatonattewa,jibungahontounikarenikouiwomotteitanokadoukamoutagawashikatta.hyottosurutoorewa,Narusetoiujinbutsuwokiniitteitanodewanakute,jibunnokangaewokouteishitekurerukareotoushite,orejishinwoaishiteitatoiudakenanokamoshirenai.soshite,kawatteshimattanaruseto,kawarenakattaoreto.tadashiinowa,tabun,narusenohounanodarou.batthingusenta-ogonishi,ekimadearuita.ho-munideruto,suguniresshagakita.shanaiwabukatsugaerinokoukouseideafureteite,orewakyuugekinitoshioitayounakibunninatta.mewotojite,resshanosoukouonnichuuiwomuketa.sudeniyoruninatteita.apa-tonimodorumaeni,konbininiyotta.chuushajouniwaoukinagagananhikimoitaga,doremougokukehaiwanakatta.bi-rutotsumamiwomotterejihemukauto,ja-jinisandarunodaigakuseinodanjogaoretoonajiyounakaimonowoshiteita.kitakushitaorewa,kanzumenoyakinikuninegiwosoeteatatametamonowotabenagarabi-ruwononda.shinumadeniatonanrittorushuwonomerunodaroutokangaeruto,bi-ruwayokeinioishikunatta.oi,kanshiinsantoorewanihanashikaketa.sakkiwa,annnakotoshitewarukatta.orewa,chottokonranshiteitandatoomou.tokidoki,kattonatte,aaiukoudounideteshimaukotogaarundaee.shittemasutowaitta.sonomeniwadokoka,orenitaisurukeikaishinnoyounamonogaukagaeta.murimonai.hanashinosaichuunitotsuzengurasuwonagetsuketekuruyounaotokonomaedewa,daredattesounaru.kegawanaika?arimasenyo.zannnennagaranaa,honkidewarukattatoomotterundayoiidesuyo.atarimasendeshitakarasonokansatsukirokutoyarawokakioetara,isshoninomanaika?aawatashitowosakewonomitai,toiukotodesuka?sonohannnouwayosoushiteinakatta.kouiutokiwashoujikinikotaetahougaiindarouna,toorewaomotta.soryamouna.sabishiikarasoudesuka.demo,moushiwakearimasenkedo,shigotochuunanodejaasaishokarasouieyosumimasen.tada,chottofushiginiomottandesu.doushitesonnnakotoiundarou,tteoredattehitonaminisabishiitokimoarusa.antagatanimitekitarenchuudatte,kitto,shinumaeniwahitokoishisounishitetadarou?oboeteimasentowaitta.bi-rukanwosubetesoranishite,atsuishawa-woabitehawomigakioerukoroniwa,kenkoutekinanemukegaotozureteita.batthingusenta-notsukarenookagedarou.akariwokeshi,futonnimoguru.douyaraninshikiwoaratameruhitsuyougaarumitaidana,toorewaomotta.ikurashikigachikaikaratoitte,sekaigakyuuniyasashikunarunadotoiukotowanainoda.sekaigayasashiinowa,osoraku,sudenishindeshimattahitonitaishitenomida.sonnnakotowawakarikitteitahazunanoni,amaetakangaeganukekiranaiorewa,kokoronodokokade,sekaigakyuuniyasashikunarukotowokitaishiteitarashii.

7.taimukapuseruarashi

izaishowokakoutoshitaorewa,donnnakotowokakunimomazu,dokushagasouteisareteinaikotoniwakakihajimerarenaitoiukotonikizuita.kinjonobunguyadekattekitabinsenwomaenipenwonigittamama,orewasokonikakubekikotonitsuitenagaikotokangaeteita.madonosotonodenchuunisemigatomatteirurashiku,heyanonakadenakareteiruyounayakamashisadatta.semigairumawafudegasusumanaikotowonakigoenoseinidekitaga,semigatobisattanochimo,orewakawarazuhitomojimokakidasezuniita.somosomoorewa,konoishogadareniyomarerukotowokitaishiteirunodarou?kotobatoiunowadentatsushudanda.oregakakukotobawa,orenonakaniarufukashinonanikao,darekanitsutaerutamenikakarenakerebanaranai.orewadareninaniwotsutaetainodarou,tojimonshitemassakiniomoiukabunowa,yahariosananajiminonokotodatta.tonaruto,orewakonoishoni,nimuketakanshanokotobayaainokokuhakuwoshirusubekinanodarouka.tameshiniorewaichijikanhodokakete,jikkuritokanojonimuketategamiwokaitemita.dekiagattasorenonaiyouwoyouyakusuruto,konnnatokoroda.imasaraomaegaorenokotowodouomooutoshittakotojanaiga,orewajuusainoanohikarazutto,omaenokotowoaishitsuzuketekita.oreganijuusaininarumadeshinazuniikitekoraretanowa,tonariniomaegaitakoronoomoidegaattakaradashi,oreganijuusaiyorisakiwoikirarezunishinunowa,tonariniomaegainaisekainitaerarenakattakarada.sonokotoniorewa,shinumaeninatteyouyakukizuita.aruimijaorewa,zuttomaekaratokkunishindeitandatoomou.omaetohanarebanareninatta,anohikara.sayounara.juusainoorega,omaenonakadesukoshidemonagakuikinobitekurerukotowonegatteiru.yomikaeshitemite,orewa,konotegamigatoukansarerukotowanaidarouna,toomotta.konotegamiwadokokadechimeitekinamachigaiwookashiteiru.oregaiitainowakonnnakotodewanai.soshite,iitaikotowoseikakunikakishirusunowafukanouda.kotobanisuruto,sorewakaetteshindeshimaudarou.orenonozomiwa,sakihodokaitabunshouno,saigonoichibunnitsukirunodatoomou.juusainoorega,nonakadesukoshidemonagakuikinobirukoto.soshitetegamiwosonomokutekinisottamononishitaitoomounonara,orewamushiro,nanimokakubekidewanainokamoshirenai.katachiarumononarananidatteyokute,tada,atenaninonamaegaatte,sashidashininniorenonamaegaareba,soredejuubunnnanoda.sochiranohougagokaiwasukunakutesumu.hakushinotegamigabukimidatoiunara,hitokoto,tegamigadashitakattatodemokakebaii.aruihajishinnoshinitsuitewaissaifurezu,dokomademotaainakunichijoutekinakotowokaku,toiutemoarudarou.penwote-burunihouridashi,niyomarenaiyounitegamiwooritatandanochi,aomukeninattetenjouwomiageta.aasorenishitemo,tegaminantekaitanowa,itsuiraidarou?kiokuwosaguru.buntsuunantemonowatouzenshitakotoganaishi,shougakuseinokorokaranengajouyarashochuumimaiwookuruaitenanteinai.jinseiotoushitemo,honnnosuutsuutoiutokorodewanaidarouka.juunanasainotokinoarewonozokuto,oregasaigonitegamiwokaitanowashougakuyonnenseinonatsuda.juusainonatsu,taiikukanuranitaimukapuseruwoumeta.reino,doutokunojugyouotsuujite,hajimeteoreniinochinokachinitsuitekangaerukikaiwoataetekuretagakkyuutannninnoteiandatta.kyuukeinokapuseruniwa,seitotachigakaitategamigairerareta.sonotegamiwa,juunengonojibunnimuketekaitehoshiindesutokanojowaitta.kyuunisonnnakotowoiwaretemo,naniwokakebaiinokawakaranaikamoshiremasenkedoaasou,tatoebayumewakanaimashitakatoka,shiawasedesukatoka,konokotowooboeteimasukatoka,gyakuni,imanowatashinitsutaetaikotowananidesukatoka,iroirokiitemirunomoiideshou.yumewokanaetekudasaitoka,shiawaseninattekudasaitokakonokotowowasurenaidekudasaitoka,youbouwotsutaerunomoiidesunekanojogayosoushinakattahazuwanai.juunengoniwasokoniitakodomonohansuuga,yumewoakirame,shiawasedewanakunari,ironnnakotowowasureteirudearoukotoo.sorewa,mirainojibunnotamenotegamidewanaku,sorewokaiteiruimanojibunnotamenotegamidattanokamoshirenai.kanojowa,koumoitta.soreto,tegaminosaigoniwa,ima,anatagaichibannotomodachidatoomotteiruhitononamaewokaiteagetekudasai.aasonotoki,namaewokakaretaaitegajibunnokotowodouomotteirukawa,anmarikinishinakuteiidesu.mukougajibunnokotowokiratteiyouto,jibunwamukounokotogasukida!ttebaaidemo,kaichattekudasai.mochironsorewa,senseimofukume,darenimomirarenaiyounigenjuuniatsukaimasukara,anshinshitekudasainejibunnimuketenaniwokaitakawa,omoidasenai.darenonamaewokaitakawa,omoidasumademonai.taimukapuseruwajuunengonihoridasarerukotoninatteita.choudokotoshida.shikashisorerashiirenrakuwanakatta.oregayobarenakattadaketoiukanouseimoaru.daga,soudenakattatoshitara.tannnirenrakugakarininatteitamonogakapuserunokotowosukkariwasureteirudakedatoshitara.aruiha,tannnimadarenrakuwosezuniirudakedatoshitara.shinumaenianotegamiwoyondemitai,toorewaomotta.tadashi,toujinokurasumeitonodaretomoaukotonaku,ichininde.kyouwadonnnakazenisugosundesuka?tachiagattaoreni,gakiku.taimukapuseruarashidatoorewakotaeta.kokyounikaerunowaichinenburidatta.purehabukoyanoyounamisuborashiiekiwoderuto,minaretakeshikigahirogatteita.midorinosakanomachi.mushinokoeyakusakinonioinokosawa,oregaimasundeirumachitowakurabemononinaranakatta.mimiwosumashitemo,kikoetekurunowatoriyamushinokoebakarida.masaka,hirumakarashougakkounishinobikondeanawohoruwakejaarimasenyone?toushirowoarukugaitta.mochiron,yorumadematsusashikashi,ikioinimakasetekokomadekitawaiiga,gorakushisetsumoinshokutenmonainihitoshiikonomachide,higaochirumadedouyattejikanwotsubusukawakangaeteinakatta.aruiteikeruhanniniwakonbinisaenainoda.konnnakotonara,jikanwokaketedemogentsukidekurebayokattanokamoshirenai.ikurajikangaamatteirukaratoitte,jikkanikaerutsumoriwanakatta.shiriaitoaunomogomendatta.jikanwomoteamashiteirundeshitara,omoidenobashodemomeguttemitaradoudesuka?wakochiranoshinjuuwominuitayouniitta.kodomonokorowahinpannikayottakedo,kokosuunenwaichidomootozureteinaibashotokaomoidenobasho,ka.konomachiniwa,iyanaomoidebakaridasannikansurukotowonozokeba,deshou?amarikarugarushikusononamaewodasanaidehoshiina.tokuni,antanokuchikarawakikitakunaindasoudesuka.igo,kiwotsukemashou.aatada,osekkaikamoshiremasenga,darekaniainiikunowayametahougaiidesuyosonotsumoriwanaiyonaraiindesukedotowasametakaodeitta.hadanitsukisasuyounahizashidatta.kyoumoatsukunarisouda.ekinosotonobenchinisuwatte,hitomazukongonohoushinwokentousurukotonishita.futotonariwomiruto,gahiyaketomerashikimonowokaradaninutteita.hajimeteattatokikarairojirodatoomott
