kagakaiteatta.chikazuitemewokorasuto,sorewayajirushidatta.yajirushinosasuhoukounimewomukeruto,kondowabetsunoyajirushigaatta.muttsunoyajirushiwokeiyushitetadoritsuitaisunouranikaiteattanowa,douyaraaiaigasarashikatta.shougakuseigafuzaketetaninnonamaewokaitari,hisokanijibuntoomoijinnonamaewokaitarisuruyouna.mochironsokonikakareteitanowa,orenonato,nonadatta.sonnnamonowokaitakiokuwanaishi,konobashowoshitteitanowaoretodakedeattakotowofumaeruto,yaharisorewadoukangaetemogakaitamonoda.kouittashoujomeitakotowosurukoniwamienakattanodaga,toorewakaowohokorobaseta.orewashibarakusonoaiaigasawonagameteita.mohaigokarasorewomiteitaga,hinikumeitakotowoiuyousuwanakatta.aiaigasawomeniyakitsukeruto,orewabasukaradete,kodomonokoronisoushiteitayouni,toubokuworiyoushitebasunoyaneninobotta.ochibayashouedawoharauto,sokoniaomukeninatta.higurashinonakihajimeruyuuguremade,soushiteita.sofunohakamairiwooe,shougakkouhemukaukoroniwayoruninatteita.nayakarasukoppuwohaishakushitekitaorewa,taiikukanuranojimeno,ouyosonokentouwotsuketehorihajimeta.hijouguchinoryokushokunoakarigaatariwobonnyaritoterashiteita.mokutekinomonowasugunimitsukarumonotoomotteitaga,douyaraorenokiokuchigaika,aruihatokkunihoridasareteshimattanoka,asedakuninatteichijikanhodohoritsuzuketemotaimukapuseruwadetekonakatta.nodogakarakaradatta.kinounobatthingusenta-noseimoatte,tewaiyoiyoboroborodatta.waoregaanawohoruyousuwominagara,no-toninanikakakikondeita.kyuukeigateratabakowosutteiruuchini,youyakukiokugamodottekita.sou,saishowataiikukanuranokinohataniumeyoutoshiteitanodaga,chikajikasokoniaratanikigauerarerukotoninarukamoshirenaitoiuhanashigahaittekite,betsunobashoniumerukotoninattanoda.kouteinobakkunettourawohoruto,juubuntotatanaiuchini,kataimononitsukiatatta.kyuukeinosorewokowasanaiyounishinchounihoridasuto,akarinohatamademotteitta.kagigakakatteirumonotoomotteitaga,suraidosasetadakedekantannihiraita.saishowa,jibunnotegamidakewotoridashite,sugumotonimodosuyoteidatta.shikashikokomadekurousaseraretakotodashi,dousenarasubetenotegaminimeotoushiteyarou,toorewakangaeta.atosuukagetsudeshinuningenniwa,sorekurainokotowayurusareruhazuda.tekitouniichimaiwotenitori,hiraku.sokonikaiteattashourainojibunhenomesse-jitoichibannotomodachinimewotousu.yomioeruto,tegamiwomotodourinishite,techouwohiraki,tegaminoarujinonamaewokaki,sokokarayajirushiwonobashite,sakiniwaichibannotomodachinonamaewokaita.nimaime,sanmaimetoyomutabini,namaetoyajirushigafueteiki,dandantosoukanzunoyounamonogadekiteitta.daregadarewosuiteite,daregadarenisukareteiruka.dokogaryouomoide,dokogakataomoika.yosouwashiteitakotodaga,kapuserunotegamiwosubeteyomioetatoki,soukanzunonakadekoritsushiteirunowa,orenonamaedakedatta.dareichinintoshite,oreoichibannotomodachiniwaerandewainakatta.soshitenotegamidakewa,ikurataimukapuserunonakawosagashitemo,mitsukaranakatta.sorewoumetanoga,tamatamakanojogagakkouwoyasundahidattanokamoshirenai.moshikanojogaitara,orenonamaewokaiteitekuretadarouni,toorewaomotta.himitsukichinihisokaniaiaigasawokakuyounakoda.kanarazuyaorenonamaewokaite,Ha-Toma-kunohitotsuyafutatsu,tsuketashitekuretadarou.notegamigaarisaesureba.sukoshimaenimitsuketeitajibunnotegamiwoji-nzunopokettonitsukkomi,taimukapuseruwoumenaoshita.sukoppuwonayanimodoshi,hatanojaguchinomizudeteyakaowoteineiniarauto,shougakkouogonishita.kutabiretashintaiwohikizutte,yomichiwoaruku.ushirokara,gaiu.iikagen,wakarimashitayone?anatawakakononingenkankeinisugarubekidewanaindesu.daiichianatawa,sorerawozutto,naigashironishitekitandesu.sangatenkoushitanochi,ichidodemo,anatanohoukarategamiwodashimashitaka?koukouwosotsugyoushitanochi,ichidodemonarusesantorenrakuwotorimashitaka?Wakanasangaanatawomikagittanowanazedesuka?dousoukainikaowodashimashitaka?aakouittewananidesukedo,imasarakakonisugarounante,mushigayosugirutoomoimasenka?sasuganiatamanikitaga,kaesukotobamonakatta.noiukotowa,tashikanitadashiinokamoshirenai.orenoshiteirukotowa,fudanwakaminanteshinjiteinaikuseni,komattatokinidakejinjayaraterayarakyoukaiyarawomeguttemisakainakukamidanomisuruyounakotonichikai.shikashi,datosurebakakomomiraimotozasaretaorewa,ittainaninisugarebaiinodarou?ekinitsuitaorewa,jikokuhyouwomitemewoutagatta.tokkunishuudennojikanwosugiteitakarada.jimotonisundeitakorowaamariresshaworiyousurukikaiganakattaga,ikurainakatowaie,kokomadekyokutannishuudenjikokugahayaitowaomotteinakatta.takushi-woyobukotomodekitashi,jikkawotayorukotomodekinaiwakedewanakattaga,saishuutekiniorewa,sonoekideichibanwosugosukotowoeranda.omouni,seishintekikutsuuganikutaitekikutsuuwouwamawatteiruyoriwa,sonogyakunohougamashinanoda.orewajibunwohodoyokuitametsukerukotode,ishikiwosochiranimukesasetakatta.kataibenchinikoshikakete,mewotojiru.mushigakeikoutounibutsukaruotoga,taemanakuhibiiteiru.shintaiwatsukarekitteirunodenemurenaitoiukotowanasasoudattaga,kounaiwaiyouniakaruku,ashimotowoironnnamushigaurotsuiteite,amarikaitekinanemuriwanozomesouninakatta.ushironobenchikarawa,gapenwohashiraseruotogakikoeta.joubunayatsuda,toorewakanshinshita.kokosuunichinoyousuwomiruni,kanojowamatomattasuimintoiumonowohotondotoranai.yachuudemo,ichifunnetegofunokiru,toittakotowokurikaeshiteirurashii.kanshiintoshitewasousuruhokanainodarouga,wakaionnnagasurushigototoshitewa,amarinikakokuda.towaie,doujousuruwakedewanai.jibungasonoyakumedenakuteyokattatoomoudakeda.

8.futekisetsunakoudou

shihatsunosuujikanmaenimewosamashitaorewa,jihankideeiyouinryouwokattenonda.karadachuugaachikochiitanda.madaatariwausuguraku,asanohigurashitokarasu,kijibatoganaiteita.kounainimodoruto,gasuwattamamanobiwoshiteita.sonoshigusawa,koremadeoregamitakanojonoshigusanonakade,mottomoningentekinamononoyounimieta.binwomottamama,orewawomitsumeteita.mushiatsuiyorudattakaraka,kanojowasama-ka-jiganwonuidehizanoueninose,kyashanashiroikatawodasukakkouninatteita.aatabun,orewakonranshiteitanodatoomou.sorewayomeisankagetsutoiujoukyounoseikamoshirenaishi,tabikasanarushitsubounoseikamoshirenaishi,neboketaatamanoseikamoshirenaishi,hirouyaitaminoseikamoshirenai.aruihatoiuonnnanokonoyoushio,jibundekangaeteiruijounikiniitteitakarakamoshirenai.nanidemoii.tonikakusonotoki,fuiniorewa,nihidoikotowoshiteyaritakunatta.mousukoshichokusetsutekiniiunaraba,wooshitaoshitakunatta.arayurukanjounohakeguchitoshite,woriyoushiteyaritakunattanoda.sorewaimanooregaomoitsukunakadewamottomofutekisetsunakouide,jikkousurebaorenojumyougatsukisaserarerukotowakakujitsudattagashikashi,dakaradoushitatoiunodarou?tattasuukagetsu,shikigahayamarudakeda.dattara,yaritaikotowoyatteshindahougaii.orewashinumaeniyaritaikotorisutonimokaitanoda,yokubounisakarawanaito.koremadewaishikishitekanojowosonotenoyokubounotaishougainioitekitaga,ichidosouiumedemihajimeruto,hodo,sonojiboujikinakouinohigaishatoshitetekisetsunaaitewainaiyouniomoeta.doushitekawashiranaiga,Miyagitoiuonnnanokowa,orenoshigyakushinwotsuyokushigekisuru.tsunenikiwohatteiruyounimierutameni,gyakunitokiorimiseruhonrainoyowasagamenitsuki,sorewoabaiteyaritakunarunokamoshirenai.antawajibunwotsuyokumisetagatteiruyoudaga,hontouhakonnnaniyowaindazotoomoishiraseteyaritakunarunoda.masshoumennitattaorewomite,wafuonnnakuukiwokanjitottanoka,migamaeruyounishiseiwotadashita.antanihitotsu,shitsumongaarundagaaahaikanshiinga,kanshitaishounofutekisetsunakoudoutoyarawokakuninshitekara,sonojumyouwotsukisaserumadenomani,dorekurainoragugaarunda?nomenikeikainoirogaukanda.doushitesonnnakotowokikundesuka?tsumari,oregaimakokode,antaniranbounankashitara,oregakorosarerumadenidorekuraikakarunokashiritainosashikashi,kanojogaodorokuyousuwanakatta.koremadeijounitsumetaimede,orewokeibetsusuruyounimitsumeta.renrakuwa,isshundesumimasu.sokokaranijuufunmokakarimasenyo.soshite,nigerukotowazettainifukanoudesujaa,juubunijouwajiyuunidekiruttewakedana?tooregasokuzanikaesuto,waorekaramewosorashi,daremosonnnakotowaittemasenyotoyowayowashiikoedeitta.chinmokugatsuzuita.fushiginakotoni,wanigedasoutoshinakatta.tada,jibunnohizawojittomitsumeteita.orewakanojonitewonobashita.baseiwoabiseraretariabareraretarisurumonotoomotteitaga,orenoteganomukidashinokatanifuretemo,kanojowakanashisounakaodeshintaiwotsuyoharasetadakedatta.korekaraorewa,woranbounihikitaoshi,yukanikumifuseshite,yokubouwokoushisurunodarou.sonosai,kanojowadokokanikegawosurukamoshirenai.anokireinahizaniaruoukinakizuo,mouhitotsufuyasukotoninarukamoshirenai.sudenihotondomakkuranakanojonomekara,saranihikariwoubaukotoninarunokamoshirenai.subetegaowattanochide,kanojowamatareinosametamedehinikuwohakunokamoshirenai,aamanzokushimashitaka?.sonnnayarikatade,orewamanzokusurunodarouka?orewananiwoshiyoutoshiteirunodarou?attoiumani,shinkeinotakaburiwanariwohisometeitta.kawariniafuretekitanowa,kyouretsunamunashisadatta.noakiramekittayounamewomiteitara,kanashimigadensenshitekitanoda.orewakaratewohanashi,kanojonofutatsutonarinisuwatta.jibunnotanrakusawohajita.taihennnashigotonandanatoorewaitta.konnnakuzunoaitewoshinakyanaranainantewaorekaramewosorashitamama,gorikaiitadaketayoude,naniyoridesutoitta.naruhodo,sanjuumanennokachimonattokuda,toorewaomotta.atoichihodeorewa,torikaeshinotsukanaikotowosurutokorodattanoda.kikennnashigotoda.oremitainayatsuwa,sukunakunaindarou?shiwomaenishiteatamawookashikushite,kanshiinniikarinohokosakiwomukeruyounayatsuwawayukkurikubiwoyokonifutta.anatawa,dochirakatoiebarakunake-sudesuyo.mottokyokutannnakoudounideruhitowa,takusanimashitakaraorenoochidowokabauyouni,souitta.deattatokikarakininatteitakanojonohizanooukinakizunitsuitetazunetakattaga,damatteirukotonishita.orenadoga,imaninattetenohirawokaeshitayounishinpaishitekitatokorode,uttoushiidakedarou.kawariniorewa,doushitekonnnashigotowoyatterunda?tokiita.kantannnaiikatawosureba,sousezaruwoenakattakaradesunekantanjanaihouwokikitaiwaigaisounakaowoshita.sanigainosonzainiwa,kyoumiganaimonotobakariomotteimashitagasonnnakotowanai.somosomooregaantanimiryokuwokanjiteinakattara,sakkimitainakoudouniwadenaisaaasoudesuka.sorewadoumohanashitakunakereba,hanasanakuteiimaa,betsunikakusuhodonokakodemonaidesukedoaaheto,jumyounohokani,kenkouto,jikangaurerukotowa,sudeniiimashitayone?orewaunazuita.tsumari,watashiwajikanwouttandesu.oyoso,sanjuunenhodosou,zuttokininatteitanoda.jikanwourutoiukotoga,naniwoimisurunoka.souka.jikanwourutteiukotowaaahai.kanshiinnotaihanwa,anatatoonajiyounianomisewootozurete,jikanwouttahitotachinandesu.kekkatekiniwa,anzenyakouyuukankeimoutteshimattayounakatachininarimashitakedosoremadewa,antamofutsuunoningendattattekotoka?hai.santoonaji,futsuunoningendeshitabakuzento,orewa,gaumaretsukireitande,umaretsukihinikuyade,umaretsukiganjounidekiteirumonodatoomoikondeita.shikashi,imanohanashiwokikuninosouittatokuchouwa,kanojogaikinokorutameni,hisshinoomoideminitsuketamonodattanokamoshirenai.antadatte,toshiwatorundarou?sanjuunenmouttara,antagakonoshigotokarakaihousarerunowa,yonjuusaikuraininattekaraka?souiukotoninarimasune.maa,soremadeikinobiraretara,nohanashidesukedotokanojowajichoumeitaemiwoukabeta.sorewakanojogakongosuujuunenkan,toumeiningendearitsuzukerukotowomoimisuru.aadoushite,sokomadeshite,kinwoeyoutoomottanda?kyouwa,shitsumongaouidesunemochiron,iyadattarakotaenakuteiianmari,omoshiroihanashijaarimasenyo?soredemo,oregajumyouwouttariyuuyoriwaomoshiroidarousawajikokuhyouwomiageta.maa,madashihatsuresshamadejikangaarimasushinetoiuto,kanojowapotsupotsutohanashihajimeta.imadaniwatashiwa,hahaga,jikanwonanjuunenmourukotomadeshitejumyouwokattariyuugayokuwakarimasen.watashigaoboeteiruhahawa,itsudattejibunnoikirugenjitsunifumanwomorashiteimashita.chichiwawatashigaumareruchokuzenniiewosattasoudesu.kotoarugotonihahawa,inakunattachichinitaisurunoroiwohaiteshimashitaga,kokoronosokodewa,kittokarenimodottekitehoshikattandatoomoimasu.aruihakarewomachitsuzukerutamedakeni,jumyouwonobasoutoshitanokamoshiremasen.mochiron,sonnnakotoshitattechichinojumyouganobiruwakedewanaishi,hahanosugatawatoumeininattedarekaramomienakunatteshimaushi,naniyori,jibunnoshintainikienaikizuwoikutsumonokoshiteittaotokonokaeriwomachinozomutoiushinriga,watashiniwarikaidekimasen.soredemomoshi,hahagachichiwomatsutameninagaikiwoshiyoutoomottanodatoshitaratabun,hontouha,sonoaitewadaredemoyokattandatoomoimasu.tada,tanisugarubekiaitegainakattatoiudakede.chichiigaini,jibunwoaishitekuresounahitowoshiranakattandeshou.aasonnnamijimenahahaga,watashiwakiraideshita.hahamowatashinokotogakiraide,kuchigusenoyounikonnnano,umanakerebayokattatomorashiteimashita.hahagajikanwouri,kanshiintonattewatashinomaekarasugatawokeshitatoki,watashiwamadarokusaidattatokiokushiteimasu.igosuunenwaobanoieniosewaninarimashitaga,sokodemowatashiwajamashaatsukaiwoukemashitasokomadehanasuto,wakangaekomuyounikuchiwotozashita.kankiwamattatoiuwakedewanasasouda.osorakukanojowa,jibunnohanasukotobaga,hakarazumodoujouwosasouyounachoushininatteshimatteirukotogakininattanodarou.tsuginokotobawa,yoritantanto,marudetaninnokotonoyounikatarareta.watashigajuusainotoki,hahawashinimashita.shiinwa,yokuwakatteimasen.tada,kanshitaishoushanikorosaretatoiunowatashikadesu.ikurajumyouwonobashitemo,gaishouyabyoukideshinunowa,matabetsumondainanodasoudesu.hajimetekiitatokiwa,sonnnanosagijanaika,toomoimashitane.aahahanoshiwoshirasenikitaotokonohitowa,mouhitotsu,juuyounakotowowatashinishirasemashita.kiminiwashakkingaaru,tokarewaiimashita.hahaoyaganokoshita,bakudainashakkinga.kimigaimasugusorewokaesuniwa,mittsushikahouhouganai.jumyouwouruka,jikanwouruka,kenkouwouruka.sonomittsudato.hahawahotondoisshoubunnojikanwourukotodejumyouwohikinobashiteimashitaga,uttabunnojikanwohatarakioerumaeni,shindeshimaimashita.kanojotoichibanchikashiitachibaniatta,musumenowatashiga,sonosekininwokoumurukotoninattatoiuwakedesu.soshite,sonobadeshakkinwokaesenakattabaai,mukougakattenimittsunouchinodorekawoerande,kyouseitekinitoritaterutonokotodeshitasorede,jikanwoerandattewakekatoorewaitta.souiukotodesu.shakkinnogakuwa,watashinojikanwosanjuunenchottourukotodekaeserukurainomonodeshita.aasouiuwakede,watashiwakouyatte,kanshiintoshiteikiteimasu.kikengaouku,kodokunashigotodesuga,sonobun,inochinokachiyahitonoikikatanitsuitewafukaichikengaeraremasu.shakkinwokaeshioetatoki,watashiwa,kittodareyorimochantoikirukotogadekirutoomoimasu.soukangaeruto,sonnnaniwaruishigotodemoarimasenyokanojowasoreo,sukuinoyounihanasu.keredomo,doukangaetemooreniwa,nojinseiwahigekisonomonotoshikaomoenakatta.wakaranainatoorewaitta.orenarasonnnajinsei,uritobasudarouna.shakkinwokaeshioerumadeikiteirareruhoshounantedokonimonaindarou?gennni,antanohahaoyawanakunatteiru.karinisaigomadeikinokottatoshite,antanojinseinoichibaniijikiwa,mouowatteshimatteirunda.korewabetsunihinikudemonanidemonaindaga,antanokotobawokarireba,sokodeyouyakusuta-tochitennitattatoiudakeda.sanzankurouwoajiwatte,yonjuusaikarayouyakuhajimarujinseittenowa,oreniwadoumohigekitoshikaomoenai.dattara,jumyouwouttahougamadaiiwatashinojumyouni,hitonaminokachigaattara,soushiteitadeshouneikuradattanda?anatatoonajidesuyowaokashisouni,souitta.ichinennitsuki,ichimanen.aawatashigaanatanihitsuyouijounitsurakuatatteshimaunowa,tabun,sonoteidonokachishikanaijibunnokotogayurusenakattakaranandatoomoimasu.dokoka,anatanijibunwokasaneteshimatteirundeshoune.yattsuataribakkarishite,gomennnasaiaakonnnakotowoiunomonanidaga,jaanaosara,sassatoshinjimattahougaiinjanainoka?toorewaitta.iyoiyomotte,sakininozomiwanaittekotojanaikaee,sonotouridesu.mattakumottesonotourinandesu.sorenanonisousezuniiruttekotowa,tsumariwatashinimo,hahaoyatoonajichiganagareteiruttekotonandeshoune.doushiyoumonaibakanandesu.ikiteitatteshikataganainoni,ikinobiyoutosezuniwairarenaindesu.hyottosuruto,shinikatamadeisshoninarukamoshiremasenne.demoaahora,yappari,kantanniwawarikiremasenyo.itsukaiikotogaarukamoshirenaijanaidesukasouiitsuzukete,gojuunenkannanihitotsuerarenaimamashindeikuyoteidattaotokonokotoo,orewaichininshitteruzetoorewajoudanwoitta.aasore,watashimoshittemasutowahohoenda.tsuraretewarainagara,orewatabakonihiwotsuketa.surutogatachiagari,orenotenonakakaratabakowoichihonhikinuite,kuchinieta.hiwotsuketeyaroutonokuchimotoniraita-wokazashitaga,choudooirugakireteshimattarashiku,nankaifurintowokosuttemochakkashinakatta.waoregaetatabakowoyubisasuto,kaowochikazuketekita.orewamukounoitowokunde,douyounikaowochikazuketa.furuerunihonnotabakonosentangafureai,jiwajiwatonotabakonihigautsutteitta.hajimeteorenomaedekatanochikarawonuitawomite,orewaomotta.semete,kanojonitotte,ichiban,hataniitekigarakudattakanshitaishoushatoshitekiokusareyou,to.senronomukougawawomitsumeru.yorugaakeyoutoshiteita.

9.dekisugitahanashi

sorekarasuunichikannoorewa,otonashiimonodatta.shokujiwosuruigainoyoudewasotonidezu,yojouhannihikikomori,bungutendekounyuushitatairyounoorigamiwote-burunikasane,hitasuratsuruwooritsuzuketa.tsukuenoueninarandaorizuruwomite,waitta.moshikashite,senbazurudesuka?aa.mitenotouridawasuujuuwanonakakaraaoiichiwawohiroiage,ryouyokuwoyubidetsumami,kyoumibukasounisorewonagameta.ichinindesenwaorutsumorinandesuka?naninotameni?shiniyukuoreno,koufukunayoseinotamenitoorewaitta.iminonaisagyouwatanoshikatta.heyawairotoridorinotsurudeumetsukusareteitta.momoironotsuru,akaironotsuru,daidaiironotsuru,kiironotsuru,kiryokushokunotsuru,ryokushokunotsuru,mizuironotsuru,aoironotsuru,murasakiironotsuru.tsuruwate-burukaraafure,kubiwofurusenpuukinitobasare,yukanichirabari,ajikenaitatamiheyawoirodotta.orewasorewomite,chottoshitamanzokukanwooboeru.muimideutsukushiikouihodo,junsuinainorigaarudarouka?tsuruwootteirusaichuu,nandomonihanashikaketakunattaga,orewanarubekujibunkarawanihanashikakenaiyounitsutometa.amari,kanojowokokoronoyoridokoronishitewanaranaitoomottakarada.souiuyarikatadeanshinwoerunowa,dokokafutounayarikatadearukigashita.shikashiippoude,nohouwajojoniorenitaisurutaidowonankasasetekiteita.megaauto,chantoshisenwosorashitekureruyouninattanoda.monowomiruyounametsukidejittomirareruyori,sochiranohougayohodoatatakaihannnoutoierudarou.senjitsunoekidenokaiwadekokorowohiraitekuretanokamoshirenaiga,aruihatannni,kanshiintoiumonowa,kanshitaishoushanojumyougachikazukunitsuretejojoniyasashikusessuruyounishijiwoataerareteirudakenanokamoshirenai.nanitoittemokanojowa,akumadeshigototoshiteorenohataniirutoiudakenanoda.sonokotowowasureteukareteiruto,itsukatehidoiuragiriwoukerudarou.gonichikakete,youyakusagyougaowatta.tsurunokazuwoaratametekazoenaoshiteiruto,jibungatsukuttanishitewaumakudekisugiteirutsurugananhikimomitsukatta.oreganeteirumani,dokokanoosekkaiyakigatsukuttanodarou.itootoushitematomeage,senbazurugakanseisuruto,orewasorewotenjoukaraburasageta.sate,tegaminohanashida.tsuruwoorioetayoru,ji-nzuwosentakushiyoutopokettononakamiwokakuninshiteiruto,oritatamaretakamigadetekita.juunengonojibunetokakaretategamidatta.taimukapuseruwohoridashitahini,pokettoniiretamamadattanoda.ji-nzuwouragaeshitesentakukinihourikomuto,ichidowamewotoushitategamio,aratameteyomikaeshita.sokoniwa,kouatta.juunengonobokue.anatanishika,tanomenaikotogaarimasu.moshimadajuunengonobokugaurenokotteiruyoudeshitara,niainiittehoshiindesu.wabokugainaitodamemitaidashi,bokuwagainaitodamemitaidakara.orewaaete,sonotegamiwonimomiseta.juunenmaenoanatawa,igaitosunaodeyasashiikodattandesunetegamiwoyondawa,kanshinshitayouniitta.sorede,dousurutsumoridesuka?niainiikuyotoorewaitta.soregadonnnaniorokashiikotonanoka,ikanimudanakotonanoka,sorosorooremorikaishihajimeteru.juunenmoattenaiosananajiminikokomadeshuuchakusurukotonobakarashisamo,juujuushouchishiteiru.demokorewa,juunenmaenoorenotanominanda.juunengonoorewa,sorewosonchoushiteyaritai.tashikani,imayoriyokeinikizutsukukotoninarukamoshirenai.imayoriyokeinishitsubousurukotoninarukamoshirenai.shikashi,konomedehakkiritomisadamerumadewa,akirameruwakeniwaikanainda.aasaigoniichidodakedemo,kanojotoattehanashigashitai.soshite,orenijinseiwoataetekuretaongaeshini,orenojumyouwoutteetasanjuumano,kanojoniwatashitaitoomounda.nanimankawa,moutewotsuketeshimattakedona.tabunwakonokotonihantaisurudarouga,orenojumyouwouttekaseidakinnanda,tsukaimichiwaorenokattedarou?watashiwatomemasenyotowaitta.sonokimochiwa,watashinimo,wakaranakuwanaidesukarakoumoassarikouteisarerutowaomowanakattanode,hyoushinukeshiteshimatta.konotokiorewa,nokuchinishitakotobanoimiwotsukitsumetekangaetariwashinakatta.shikashi,nochiniorewasonokotobawoomoikaeshite,sokodeyouyakuhontounoimiworikaisuru.waorenokimochigawakaranakuwanaidokorodewanakatta.mushiro,kanojowasonokimochiwoshitteitanoda.oreyorimo,zuttomaeni.ashitanoasanidemo,noieniittemiyoutoomou.aitsu,imawajikkaniirundarou?soudesune.ottotowakaretekarawa,zuttojikkawotayotteirumitaidesusouittanochi,wakaoirowoukagauyouniuwamezukaideorenomewomita.nitsuiteorenomaedekatarukotoniteikougaarunodarou.matarifujinniharawotaterarerunodewanaikatoshinpaishiteirunoda.sokodeorewa,henimonakuarigatoutoitta.douitashimashitetowaandoshitayouniitta.tenkyogononojuushowooregashitteitawakewosetsumeishiyoutoomottara,mazu,juunanasainonatsunikaraorenomotohetodoita,ichitsuunotegaminitsuitehanasanakerebanaranai.sorewoyondaorewa,iiyounonaiiwakanwooboeta.dounimokareonnnarashikunaitegamidana,toorewaomotta.sokonikakareteitanowa,taainonaikotodatta.jukenbenkyougaisogashikutehonwoyomuhimasaenaikoto,konotegamimobenkyounoaimawonuttenankainimowaketekaiteirukoto,mezashiteirudaigakunokoto,fuyuyasuminiichido,kochiraniasobinikurukamoshirenaitoiukoto.ikanimojuunanasainoonnnanokogakakisounakotoga,juunanasainoonnnanokogakakisounamaruijide,kakareteita.shikashi,dakarakosookashiinoda.sorewokaitanogaheibonnnajuunanasainoonnnanokodattara,nanimomondaiwanai.shikashi,konkaitegamiwokaiteokuttekitanowa,anonanoda.orenimakezuotorazunejikureteiruhazuno,heibontowahodotouionnnanokoda.sorenanoni,hinikunohitotsumomiataranakereba,batounomonkumonaitowadouiukotodarou?kussetsushikittawadokoheitteshimattanda?juunanasainimonaruto,sorenarinihitomokawarutoiukotodarouka?soretomotannni,shaberunotokakunotodewakattegachigautoiudakede,bunmendewafutsuunokotoonajiyounifurumaukodattanodarouka?gimonnitaisurutekisetsunakotaewomitsukerarenaimama,nishuukango,orewaokuraretekitategamitonitayounanaiyounotegamiwokaeshita.kochiramojukenbenkyougaisogashikuhenshinnitemadotteshimattakoto,mezashiteirudaigakunokoto,gaasobinikurebaureshiitoiukoto.orewahenjiwomachitsuzuketaga,yokushuuninattemo,yokugetsuninattemo,karanotegamiwakaettekonakatta.fuyuyasuminigaasobinikurutoiukotomonakatta.orewananikamachigaiwookashiteshimattanodarouka?shikashi,toujinooretoshitewa,soutounamuriwoshite,shoujikinitoaitaitoiukimochiwosokonikaitatsumoridatta.kakikatagayokunakattanodarouka,tosonotokiwakangaeta.dagaosorakusonokoroniwa,watokkuni,orenoshiranaidarekanokowoharaniyadoshiteitanodarou.juuhachisaidekekkonshi,yokunenniwarikonsurukotoninaruaiteno 10.watashino,tattahitorinoosananajimie

11.jihankimegurinosusume

kouminkankarayonjikanarukitsuzuke,youyakuapa-tonitsuita.jishitsunonioiganatsukashikatta.karadachuuasemamirede,ashiwamamedarakedatta.shawa-woabiyoutoshitedatsuishonotobirawoaketatokorode,futo,sakininitsukawasetahougaiidarouka,tokangaeta.shikashiamarikiwotsukaisugiruto,gaitoshitetsukuriagetekitakyorikano,kochirakarahakaisurukotoninatteshimaukamoshirenai.yuwoabitsuzuketeitainowogamanshite,tebayakukaradawoarai,kigaewosumaseteimanimodotta.koremadenokeikenkaraitte,gajiyuuninyuuyokuyashokujigadekirunowa,oreganeteirumanominoyoudatta.dakaraorewafutonniyokotawari,sassatoneteshimaukotonishita.mewotojitenetafuriwoshiteiruto,gakosokosotoshawa-woabiniikuotogakikoeta.shintaiwookosoutosuruto,futatabikanojogamodottekuruashiotogashitanode,awatetemewotojita.santowaitta.orewakizukanaifuriwoshita.san,neterundesuka?towaorenomakuramotomadekite,kogoedeitta.konnnakotowokikunowa,mochiron,anatagatanukineirishiteiruyounimierukaradesu.soshite,moshianatagasonnnakotowosurunoga,watashiwokizukattenokotodattaraiinonina,toomoimasu.aaoyasuminasai.shawa-,karimasunedatsuishonodoagashimaruotogasuruto,orewaokiagari,gainaiheyanosumiwonagameta.kyoumokanojowaasokodenemurunodarouka.anosukoshimoyasumarisouninaitaiseide,suufunokitekanshiniatattewasuufunnerukotowokurikaesunodarouka.tameshinisonoichinisuwari,noshiseiwomaneshiteneyoutoshitemita.shikashiikuramattemo,nemuriwayattekonakatta.modottekitagaorenokatawohataki,nandekonnnatokoroniirundesuka.futondenetahougaiidesuyotosatosuyouniitta.sorewakotchinodaishidayo.antakosofutondenetahougaii.konnnatokorodenerunante,yappariokashiiokashikutekekkoudesuyo.watashiwanareterukaraiindesuorewafutonniyokotawaruto,hidarihashiniyotta.korekaraorewafutonnohidarihashideneru.mounanigaattemomigigawaniwashinnnyuushinaishi,mimoshinai.sokowaorewochikakudekanshisurunoniuttetsukenobashodarouna.tsukaunomotsukawanainomonokattedaga,tonikakuorewahidarihashidenerusoregadakyoutendatta.osorakuwa,oregayukadenetekanojogafutondenerutoiuyounajoukenwa,zettaininomanaidarou.tonaridenetemoiitooregaitte anatanimoshumikuraiarudeshou?aa.ongakukanshouto,dokushogasoredatta.aashikashi,imakangaeruto,konofutatsuwaorenitotte,ikiteikutamenoshudandattanda.doushiyoumonaijinseitooriaiwotsukerutameni,ongakutohonwomochiiteitandayo.muriniikiteikuhitsuyouganakunattaima,sonofutatsuwaorenitotte,izenhodojuuyoudewanakunattekiterukanshouhouhouwokaerebaiijanaidesuka.kondowajunsuinisonoutsukushisawotanoshimebaiindesuyodemo,doushitemohikkakatchimaundayona.naniwomikikishitemo,aa,korewaoretowakankeinonaihanashinandattesogaikanwooboerunda.aaomouni,yononakanotaiteinomonowa,kongomoikitsuzukeruhitomukinitsukurareteirundayo.touzentoieba,touzendaga.korekarashinuhitonotameniwatsukurareteinaitonarideushidonburiwokakikondeirugojuusaikurainootokoga,ichinindeshinitsuitekataruorewomitemayuwoshikameteita.mottosobokunisukinakotowanaindesuka?sono,tatoeba,haikyowomirunogasukidatoka,senronomakuragiwokazoetearukunogasukidatoka,juunenmomukashinimisuteraretayounage-mukatamitaideasobunogasukidatokayakenigutaitekidana.hyottoshite,imamadenokanshitaishoushani,souiuhitogaitanoka?hai.tanimo,soukouchuunokeitorakkunonidaininesobette,sorawomiagerukotonisaigonoichikagetsuwotsuiyashitahitonankamoimashita.jumyouwoutteetakino,mizushirazunoroujinnisokkurisonomamawatashite,hitonimitogamerarenaitokorodekeitorakkuwohashirasetsuzuketehoshiitotanondandesunodokanahanashidana.demoangai,souiunogaichibankashikoiyarikatananokamoshirenaikekkou,omoshiroimononandesuyo.keshikigaushironitondeiku,anokanjigashinsendeorewasonoyousuwosouzoushitemita.aozoranoshita,semakumagarikunettainakamichio,kokochiyoikazetoshindouwokanjinagara,dokomademoyukuime-ji.omoidemokoukaimo,subeteatamaniukandasonobakara,douroniochiteokizarinisareteiku.nanimokamogasusumebasusumuhodohanareteikutoiukankakuwa,shiniyukuningenniyokuniau.souiuhanashi,mottokikasetekurenaika.shokugyourinritokashuhigimutoka,souiumononihikkakaranainodearebatoorewaitta.apa-tonimodottara,ikurademohanashimasuyotowaitta.tada,kokodeitsumademohanashiteruto,ayashimaremasunodekaerimichiwaoukikutoumawa 12.usotsukitochisananegai

gakanshiintoshitekonoapa-towootozuretatousho,orewakanojonoshisengakininatteshikataganakatta.moshikanshiinga,konoonnnanokototaishoutekina,minikukufutottafuketsunachuunennadodeareba,orewamottorirakkusushite,jibunnoyaritaikotonitsuiteshoujikinikangaerukotogadekitadarou,souomottamonodatta.ima,nokawariniorenomaeniirukanshiinwa,masanisonoyounaotokodatta.sewahikuku,touhatsuwamigurushikuhageagari,kaowayopparainoyouniakarandeirukusenihigewaaoaotoshiteori,hadawaaburagitteita.mewafushizennimabatakigaouku,hanaikiwaaraku,nodonookunitangakaramatteiruyounashaberikatawoshita.itsumonokowa?oregasaishonitazunetanowa,soredatta.yasumidatootokowabukkirabounikotaeta.kyoutoashitawa,oregadairidaorewamunewonadeoroshita.kanshiingakoutaiseidenaikotonikanshashita.ninichimateba,matawamodottekurunoda.kanshiinnimo,kyuujitsugaarundanatoorewaitta.soryaahitsuyousa.omaetochigatte,kongomozuttoikiteikanakinaraneendakaranatootokowaiyamitarashikuitta.souka.sorewa,anshinshita.myougonichiniwakyuujitsugaowatte,motonimodorundana?ichiou,souiuyoteiniwanatterutootokowakotaeta.nebokemewokosuri,aratameteheyanosuminiiruotokonosugatawomiruto,karewaorenoarubamuwotenitottenagameteita.koremadetottekitajihankinoshashingahaitteiruarubamuda.ittai,koryananinanda?tootokowaorenikiita.jidouhanbaikimoshiranainoka?toorewatoboketeyatta.otokowashitauchiwoshita.naninotamenikonnnashashinwototterunoka,tokiitatsumoridattandagasoragasukinayatsugasorawototari,hanagasukinayatsugahanawototari,denshagasukinayatsugadenshawototarisurunotoonajidayo.toritaikaratotteru.orewajihankigasukinandaotokowaarubamuwotaikutsusouninanpe-jikamekuri,gomidanatoitteoreninageteyokoshita.soshiteatarinichirabatteiruboudainakazunoorizuruwonagamete,wazatorashikutameikiwotsuita.konnnakotoniyoseiwotsuiyashiterunoka.kudaranee.mottomashinasugoshikatawanainoka?karenotaidowa,sorehodoorewofukainisasenakatta.omottakotowosotchokuniittemoraerunowa,kangaeyouniyottewakigarakudatta.heyanosumikaramonoiitagenamedemitsumeraretsuzukeruyoriwa,zuttoii.arukamoshirenaiga,koreijoutano anojonoshakkinwozenbukaeshiteyaritai.souomotta.isshougakanju-suichihonnonedannimitanaikonoorega,da.minohodoshirazutowa,kouiukotowoiunodarou.

13.tashikanakoto

hanashiwajojoniowarinichikazuiteiru.oregakonokirokunisakerujikanmosukunakunattekita.konomamadewasaigomadekakikirerukadoukamoSatoshitabanai.jojonibunshounomitsudowosageteikazaruwoenaikotoo,zannnenniomou.noshakkinwohensaisurukotoniyoseiwosasageruketsuiwoshitaoredattaga,kentouchigaibakarisuruorokasawa,soukantanninaorumonodewanakatta.dagakokokarasakinohanashinikagitteieba,orenokentouchigaiwasokomadesemerarerumonodemoarumai.somosomo,zenteikaraittemurinoaruhanashinanoda.noshakkinwa,katsutenoitteitasarari-mannoshougaichinginwokaniuwamawarugakudatta.soredakenokingakuwoheibonnnadaigakuseiganikagetsudekasegunoni,touwoetayarikatanadohajikarasonzaishinainoda.soredemohitomazu,kentouwashitemita.jimichinihatarakoutoiushushounakangaekatawa,konobaainikagittewahigenjitsutekidatta.donnnanikenmeinihataraitatokorode,nikagetsuteidoshikahatarakenainodearebayakeishinimizuda.gakuretasanjuumanwokaesukuraiwadekirudarouga,oregasonotamedakeniyoseiworoudounitsuiyasukotowokanojoganozomutowaomoenakatta.douyouni,settou,goutou,sagi,yuukaitoittahanzainioregatewosomerukotomo,wanozomanaidarou.kanojonotamenikasegunodakarakoso,kanojoganozomanaihouhoudekaseguwakeniwaikanakatta.kakegototoiutemokangaetaga,sasuganooremo,sorewohonkidejikkousuruhodonobakadewanakatta.kouiuseppatsumattajoukyoudenogyanburuwamazukatenainodatoiukotoo,orewayokushitteita.itsudattekakegotowa,Kimugaamatteiruningengakatsumonoda.kouunnomegamiwa,kochirakaratewonobasutonigeteshimau.mukoukarachikazuitekurunowoshinbouzuyokumatte,kokozotoiutaimingudetsukamaerumonoda.shikashioreniwasorewomatteirudakenoyoyuuwanakattashi,sonotaiminguwokagitorudakenokyuukakuwosomosomomochiawaseteinakatta.kumowotsukamuyounahanashida.nikagetsudeisshoubunkaseguhouhou,sonnnasubarashiimonogaarunara,daremogatokkunijikkoushiteiru.orenoyatteirukotowa,minagahakkiritofukanoudearutoshoumeishitakotoo,wazawazamouichidoshoumeishiyoutoiudakenokotonisuginai.orenoyuiitsunobukitoieba,yoseigamijikaidakenidonnnarisukudemooerutoiutendattaga,jinseiwonageuttedemokinwokasegitaitoomottan ewaomotta.jikanwomihakarai,sorosoroikanaikatokogoedeiuto,wakubiwoyokonifutta.arigatougozaimasu.demo,miteokitaindesu.karegaimaaishiteirunoga,donnnahitonanokaniryouhenseinoresshagatouchakushita.oritekurukyakunotaihanwakoukouseidattaga,ichinin,kanjinoyoinijuudainakabanojoseigaita.soregaenishinomachibitodearukotowa,kareragashinmitsunaemiwokawashiaumaekarayosoudekiteitakotodatta.totemoshizennnawaraikatawosurujoseidatta.shizensugite,gyakunifushizennnakuraidatta.hitonoegaotoiumonowa,futsuu,donnnanishizennidetekitawaraidemodokokatsukurimonomeiteirumonodaga,enishinokoibitodearusonojoseinoegaoniwa,souiufushizensagaissainakatta.sorewajunsuinaemidakewoukabetsuzuketaseikananokamoshirenai.kotobawokawasazushizennigouryuushitatokorowomiruni,tsukiaiwamijikaimonodewanasasoudattaga,tagainokaowomitashunkannoureshikuteshikatanasasounahyoujouwa,marudehajimetemachiawasewosurunininnoyoudatta.tattanosuubyounokotodattaga,kareragakoufukudearukotowoshiruniwa,soredejuubundatta.enishiwagainakutomo,shiawaseniyatteita.wanakimowaraimosezu,muhyoujouninininwomitsumeteita.douyoushiteitanowa,mushirokochiranohoudattakamoshirenai.orewaenishitosonokoibitonosugatani,oretonosugatawokasaneteita.hyottoshitaraarietakamoshirenai,odayakadeshiawasenamiraio,isshuntowaieomoiegaiteshimatta.oregashinazunisundakamoshirenakattamiraio.niningasari,kounainiwaoretodakeganokotta.hontouha,mukougamienainowoiikotoni,iroiroshiteyaroutoomottetandesuyotokanojowaitta.demo,yamemashitatatoeba,donnnakotoo?toorewakiita.muriyaridakitsukutoka,sonnnakotosonnnakotoka.oregaonajitachibadattara,soreijounokotowoshitetadarounatatoeba?togaiioeruyorisakiniorewakanojonokoshiwoidakiyose,soreijounokotowojissenshitemiseta.nibunkurai,soushiteita.hajimewaodoroitemiwokatakushiteitadattaga,jojoniochitsuitekuruto,mukoukaramokotaetekureta.youyakukuchibiruwohanashitatokorode,orewaitta.dousedarenimotogamerarenaindattara,korekuraijibungattenakotowoshiteyarusaaasoudesune.daremo,togamemasenutsumuitamama,wayattonokotodesouitta.

14.aonojidai

henkagahakkiritokatachininattearawaretanowa,orenojumyougagojuunichiwokittakoronokotodatta.senjutsushitayouni,orenoboujakubujinkatsuhatawakayuujinnakoudouni,kennokanwoshimesuhitowataiseiita.toumeiningennimukatteshiawasesounikatarikakeruorewomite,tonarinoningentomimiuchishiauhitotachiya,kochiranikikoeruhodonoougoedehidoikotowoiuhitotachimosukunakunakatta.muron,monkuwoiukenriwakochiraniwanai.sakinifukaikanwoataetanowaorenohounanodakara.sonohi,orewaizakayadesanninnootokonikaramareta.yatarakoegaoukiku,itsudemomezatokujibunwotsuyokumiserukikaiwoukagatteite,aitenoninzuutotaikakuwomitauedekougekitekinataidowotorukadoukawoshinchounikimeruyounarenchuuda.taikutsushiteitanodarou,ichinindesakewonominagarakuusekinimukatteshaberikaketeiruorewomiruto,wazawazamayokonisuwattekite,chouhatsutekinakotobawonagekaketekita.izennoorenarabaijiwohattenanikaiikaeshiteitakamoshirenaiga,imanoorewamousouiukotonienerugi-wosakoutowaomoenakattanode,mukougaakirunowoshinbouzuyokumatta.shikashioregananimoyarikaeshitekonaikotogawakaruto,renchuuwatsukeagari,saranitaidowooukikushitekita.misewoderukotomokangaetaga,ikanimojikanwomoteamashiteisounatokorowomiruni,sonomamatsuitekiteshimaukamoshirenai.komarimashitane,togaorewoshinpaisuruyounakaodeitta.doushitamonokatooreganayandeitasonotoki,haigokaraare,sanjanaidesukatoiukoegashita.otokonokoedatta.jibunnisonnnakazenihanashikakeruotokonikokoroatariganakattaorewa,soredakedemojuubunniodoroitanodaga,tsuzuitekaregahasshitakotobaniwa,oremomogyoutenshiteshibarakukuchigakikenakatta.kyoumo,santoisshonandesunefurikaette,koenoarujinosugatawomiru.menshikinonaiotokodewanakatta.sorewaapa-tonotonariheyanisundeiruotokodatta.itsumotohanashinagaraheyawodeirisuruorewomite,kimiwarusounakaowoshiteitaotoko.tashika,Shinbashitoiunamaedattahazuda.shinbashiwaorenimukattemassuguaruitekuruto,sokoniitarenchuunoichininnimukatte,moushiwakearimasenkedo,sonoseki,yuzuttemoraemasenka?toitta.kotobawateineidattaga,kuchouwakouatsutekidatta.sekiwoyuzuruyouiwaretaotokowa,shinbashinoyuunihyakuhachijuusenchiwokoerutaikakutohitowoodosunoninaretayounametsukiwomitatotan,rokotsunitaidowokaeta.orenotonarinisuwattashinbashiwa,orenidewanaku,nimukatteitta.anatanohanashiwaitsumosankarakiiterundesuga,jissainihanashitakotowaarimasendeshitane.hajimemashite,shinbashitoiimasuwaakkenitoraretakaodekouchokushiteitaga,karewamarudegananikashiranohenjiwoshitakanoyouniunazuita.ee,soudesu.oboetekureteitandesuka,koueidesu.bokurawaapa-tonomaedenandomosurechigatterundesuyokaiwawaseiritsushiteinai.toiukotowa,shinbashiwajissaininosugatagamieteirutoiuwakedewanairashii.hyottosuruto,konootokowa,gamieteirufuriwoshitekureteirunodarouka,toorewaomou.sakihodomadeorenikarandeitarenchuuwa,shinbashinotoujoudeyarukiwonakushitarashiku,kaerijitakuwohajimeteita.sanningamisewoderuto,shinbashiwakaruitameikiwotsuki,soremadekaoniharitsuketeitashakoutekinaemiwosute,itsumonokigennowarusounakaonimodotta.sakiniitteokimasukedotoshinbashiwaitta.bokuwabetsuni,honkidesonotokaiuonnnanokogairukotowoshinjiteiruwakejaarimasenyowakatterusa.tasuketekuretandarou?toorewaitta.kanshasuruyo.arigatoutokorogasouiuwakedemonaindesuyotokarewakubiwoyokonifuru.jaadouiuwakeda?anatawakesshitemitomenaideshougasukunakutomobokuwa,koukangaeteimasu.anatanoyatteirukotowaarutanenopafuo-mansude,ikanioukunohitoni,sonotoiuonnnanokogajitsuzaisuruyounasakkakuwoidakaserarerukanichousenshiteiru.kanzennnapantomaimuniyottetashanoninshikiwoyuragaserarerukotowoshoumeishiyoutoshiteiru.aasoshitesonokokoromiwa,bokunitaishitewa,sokosokoseikoushiteimasusorewa,nosonzaiwoaruteidokanjirareru,ttekotoka?mitometakuwaarimasenga,souiukotoninarimasutoitteShinbashiwakatawosukumeta.sonotsuideniitteshimauto,bokuwakonjibunnonakaniokiteiruhenkani,asakaranukanshingaarundesu.konochoushide,anatagabokunikanjisaserusannosonzaiwosekkyokutekiniukeireteittara,sonouchi,kanojonosugatagajissainimieruyounisaenatteshimaunjanaika,ttewa,toorewaitta.amarisewatakakunai.irojirode,dochirakatoiebakyashanaonnnanokoda.fudanwasametamewoshiteiruga,tamanihikaemenaegaowomisetekureru.megasukoshiwaruinoka,komakaimojiwomiruyounatokiniwahosoifure-munomeganewokakerundaga,soregahontouniyokuniaunda.kamiwasemirongude,uchimakinokusegaaruaadoushitedeshoune?toshinbashiwakubiwokatageta.imaanataganarabetatokuchou,ichikarajuumade,bokunosouzoushitasannosugatasonomamanandesuyososhiteima,waantanomenomaeniiru.doushitedatoomou?shinbashiwamewotojitekangaeru.sokomadewawakarimasenneakushuwomotometerundayotoorewaitta.migitewomaenidashitekurenaika?karewahanshinhanginohyoujoude,migitewomaenisashidashita.sonoteo,waureshisounimitsume,ryoutedenigitta.jougeniyusaburarerujibunnotewomite,shinbashiwaitta.korewatabun,sangatewoyusabutteiru,toiukotonandesune?aa.antawajibundeyusabutteirutoomotteirudarouga,jissaiwagaantanotewonigitteyusabutterunosa.soutouyorokondeirumitaidaarigatougozaimasu,toshinbashisannitsutaetekuremasuka?togaitta.gaarigatougozaimasutotsutaetekuretoitterutoorewadaibenshita.nantonaku,soudaroutoomoimashitayotoshinbashiwafushigisouniitta.douitashimashitesonogo,orewobaikaitoshite,toshinbashinomadeikutsukanokotobagakawasareta.motonote-burunimodorumaeni,shinbashiwamouichidohikikaeshitekite,orenikouitta.anatanotonarinisannosonzaiwokanjiteirunowa,osoraku,bokudakedewanaihazunandesu.mina,ittanwanitayounakankakuwoidakitsutsumo,sorewokudaranaisakkakudearutojishinniiikikaseteirundatoomoimasu.shikashi,nanikanokikkakesaearebatatoebakareraga,soushitasakkakuwodaiteirunogajibundakedenaitoshirukotogadekirebaangai,attoiumani,daremogasannosonzaiwoukeireruyouninarunodewanaideshouka.aamochiron,naninokonkyomonaihanashidesu.tada,bokuwasounarukotowonegatteimasushinbashinoyosouwatadashikatta.shinjigataikotodaga,konokenwokikkakeni,nosonzaigashuuinoningenniukeirerarehajimetanoda.mochironmina,toumeiningennosonzaiwohonkideshinjitawakedewanai.orenotawagotoo,kyoutsuunoyakusokugototoshiteatsukai,hanashiwoawasetekureruyouninattatoiudakeda.nosonzaigakasetsunoikiwoderukotowanakattaga,sorenishitemo,oukinahenkadearukotonichigaiwanai.machinogorakushisetsuyakoukounobunkasai,jimotonomatsurinadohinpannikaowodashiteir rou.shikashi,sorenonanigaikenaitoiunodarou?kononatsu,orewakonomachide,ichibannodoukedatta.yokumo,warukumo.sorekaranannichikagasugita,haretahinogogonokotoda.yobiringanari,shinbashinokoegakikoeta.doawoakerunari,karewaorenimukattenanikawohourinagetekita.tenohirawoaketeuketottasorewomiruto,jidoushanokagidatta.jikkanikaerundesutoshinbashiwaitta.dakara,orenisorewa,shibarakuhitsuyounaindesuyo.yokattarawokashishimasu.santoisshoni,umidemoyamademominiittaradoudesu?orewanandomokarenireiwoitta.kaerigiwa,shinbashiwakouitta.yapparibokuniwa,anatagatadausowotsuiteiruyouniwamienaindesu.sannosonzaigapantomaimuniyottetsukuridasaretamonodatowa,totemoomoenai.aaaruihajissaini,anatanishikamieteinaisekaigaarunokamoshiremasenne.bokutachigamiteirusekaiwa,konosekainoshinjitsuniokeruhonnnoichibu,jibuntachinitottesoresaemieteirebaiitoiububunnisuginainokamoshiremasenbasuninottekaetteittakarewomiokuttanochi,orewasorawomiageta.menokuramuyounahizashiwaaikawarazudattaga,tadayoukuukinonakani,honnnoritoakinonioigakagitoreta.tsukutsukuboushigaisseininaki,natsuwoowaraseyoutoshiteita.yoruninatte,orewatoisshonifutonnimogutta.kyoukaisenwaitsunomanikanakunatteita.waoretomukaiattenemutta.suusuuneikiwotatete,kodomomitainiyasurakanakaode.sononegaowanandomitemonarenaishi,akinaishi,aioshikatta.kanojowookosanaiyounisottofutonkaradete,daidokorodemizuwonondeheyanimodoroutoshitatoki,datsuishonotobiranomaeni,reinosuketchibukkugaochiteirunowomitsuketa.orewasorewohiroiageruto,nagashidainokeikoutouwotsuke,sottoichipe-jimewohiraita.souzoushiteitaijouni,samazamanamonogasokoniwaegakareteita.ekinomachiaishitsu.narusetoattaresutoran.taimukapuserunoumeteattashougakkou.toorenohimitsukichi.senbazurugasanranshitaheya.furubitatoshokan.natsumatsurinoyatai.toauzenjitsunioretodearuitakawabe.tenboudai.ninindenetomarishitakouminkan.kabu.dagashiya.jihanki.koushuudenwa.hoshinomizuumi.koshoten.suwanbo-to.kanransha.soshite,orenonegao.orewaaratanape-jiwomekuri,shikaeshini,nonegaowoegakihajimeta.nemukedeatamagaboyaketeitaseika,jibungasaigom 15.kanjanomegurimono

nokorisannichi,saishonoasadatta.kokokarawa,kanshiinnomewaissainai.wa,mouinaitoiukotoda.sonosannichikanwodouyattesugosukawa,tokkunikimeteita.gozenchuuwa,no-tohenokakikominitsuiyashita.kinoumadenodekigotowokakioeruto,mannnenhitsuwooite,suujikangussurinemutta.megasameruto,sotonidetetabakowosui,jihankidesaida-wokattekawaitanodowouruoshita.orewaaratametesaifuwomita.hyakuhachijuunanaen.soredezenbudatta.shikamo,sonouchirokujuuenwasubeteichiendamada.sankaikazoetemitaga,yapparihyakuhachijuunanaendatta.kimyounaguuzennikizuki,orewahouwoyurumeta.sannichikanwosugosuniwashoushoukokoromotonaiga,imawasonoguuzenwotanoshimou.no-towominaoshitehitsuyounasaibuwotsuketasuto,orewakabunimatagari,katsutetoisshonimeguttabashoo,kondowaichinindemegutta.sokoniarukanojononokoriganoyounamonowomotomete,aozoranoshitawohashiritsuzuketa.waimagoro,dokokadeoretowabetsunodarekawokanshishiteirunodarou.soitsugajikininattewoosotarishinaikotoo,orewainotta.kanojogajunchounihatarakitsuzuke,shakkinwokaeshioetanochi,orenokotonadowasureteshimaukurainishiawasenamainichiwosugoseruyou,orewainotta.nitotteoreyoritaisetsuniomoete,katsuoreyorimowotaisetsuniomoeruhitogaarawarerukotoo,orewainotta.kouenwoaruiteiruto,kodomotachigaorenimuketetewofuttekita.orewafutoshitaomoitsukide,gairufuriwoshitemirukotonishita.tewosashidashite,hora,toitte,kuusoujounototewotsunagu.mawarikaramireba,sorede,itsumotourinokoukeidattanodarou.aa,matanobakagakakuunokoibitotoaruiteruyotodemoomowaretakotodarou.shikashi,orenitottewadaichigaidatta.amarinimonanimokamogachigatteita.orewasorewojibunkarayatteokinagara,matomonitatteirarenaihodonokanashiminiosowareta.nofuzaio,koreijounaihodokyouretsunijikkanshiteshimatta.futo,orewaomou.hyottoshitara,saishokara,subetewaorenomitamaboroshidattanodewanaidarouka.jibunnoisshougaatosannichideowarutoiukakushinwaaru.inochinokakerasaehotondomoyashitsukushiteshimattanogawakaru.sonokankakudakewa,usodewanaidarou.shikashi,Miyagitoiuonnnanokowa,hontounijitsuzaishiteitanodarouka?kanojonosonzaiwa,iyasoredokoroka,jumyouwokai atogaki

bakawashinumadenaoranaitoiukotobagaarimasuga,bokuwakorenitsuitemousukoshirakkantekinamikatawoshiteorimashite,bakawashinumadeniwanaorudaroukurainikangaeteimasu.hitokuchinibakatoittemojitsunisamazamanashuruinobakagasonzaishimasuga,kokodebokunoiubakawa,mizukarajigokuwotsukuridasuhitobitonokotodesu.soushitabakanotokuchoutoshite,mazu,jibunwashiawaseninarenaitotsuyokuomoikondeiru,toiutengaageraremasu.yorijuudoninaruto,sonoomoikomiwajibunwashiawaseninarubekidewanainimadekakuchousare,saishuutekiniwajibunwashiawaseninaritakunaitoiuhametsutekinagokainiitarimasu.kounarutomou,kowaimonowaarimasen.karerawafukouninarushudantoiumonowojukuchishiteori,donnnanimegumaretakankyoudearouto,kanarazunukemichiwomitsukedashite,kiyounikoufukuwokaihishitemisemasu.ichirennokateiwasubetemuishikikadeokonawarerutame,karerawakonoyonosubetegajigokudatoomotteimasugajissainotokoro,kareragasusunde,jibunnoirusokowojigokunishiteirutoiudakenanodesu.bokujishinsoushitajigokunotsukurishunoichinindakarakosokakushinwomotteierunodesuga,koushitabakawa,sousounaorumonodewaarimasen.fukounajibungaaidenthithininattamononitotte,fukoudenakunarukotowa,jibundenakunarukotodesu.fukounitaerutameniitteitajikorenbinwaitsushikayuiitsunotanoshimitonari,sonotamenofukouwosekkyokutekinisagashiniikuyounisaenarimasu.desuga,boutoudenobetatouri,bokuwakoushitabakao,shinumadeniwanaorumonotokangaeteirunodesu.yoriseikakuniieba,shinochokuzenninatte,hajimetenaorudaroutoiunogabokunokangaedesu.kouunnnahitowasounarumaeninaorukikkakewoerarerukamoshiremasenga,tatoefuunnnahitodemo,jishinnoshigasakerarenaimonodearutojikkantekinisatori,konosekaideikitsuzukenakerebanaranaitoiushigaramikarakaihousaretasonotokiyouyaku,bakakarakaihousarerunodewanaideshouka.bokuwakonomikataworakkantekitoiimashitaga,yokuyokukangaerutokorewa,soutounihikantekitomoiemasu.sekaiwohajimeteaiseruyouninattakoroniwa,karenoshiwaketteitekidearu,toiuwakedesukara.tada,bokugaomouni,soushitabakawanaottaga,mouteokurenokarenomeotoushitemirusekaiwa,tabun,subetegadoudemoyokunatteshimaukuraini,utsukushiinodesu.orewa,konnnanimosubarashiisekainisundeitanoni,imanooreniwa,subetewoukeireteikirukotogadekirunonitoittakoukaiyanagekigafukerebafukaihodo,sekaiwakaette,zankokunakurainiutsukushikunarunodewanaideshouka.souiuutsukushisanitsuitekakitaito,bokuwatsunezunekangaeteimasu.konosannichikannokoufukuniseyo,sakuhinotoushiteinochinokachidatokaainochikaradatokanitsuitekataroutoiukiwa,miwoiuto,sarasaranainodesu.
